React 19 中 和 <meta> 的自动管理：Document Metadata 的演进 / React 19 Document Metadata 是怎么工作的？之前为什么要用 react-helmet？</h3><p><strong>标准答案</strong>：</p> <p>React 19 内置了 Document Metadata 支持——<strong>直接在组件中渲染 <code><title></code>、<code><meta></code>、<code><link></code> 标签，React 会自动将它们提升（hoist）到 <code><head></code> 中</strong>：</p> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span function_">useEffect</span>(<span class="function">() =></span> {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="variable language_">document</span>.<span class="property">title</span> = title;</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> meta = <span class="variable language_">document</span>.<span class="title function_">querySelector</span>(<span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"><<span class="name">title</span>></span>{post.title} | My Blog<span class="tag"></<span class="name">title</span>></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"><<span class="name">meta</span> <span class="attr">name</span>=<span class="string">"description"</span> <span class="attr">content</span>=<span class="string">{post.excerpt}</span> /></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="attr">posts</span>/${<span class="attr">post.slug</span>}`} /></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"><<span class="line">}</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>之前为什么需要 react-helmet？</strong></p> <ul> <li>React 18 及之前，React 不会将 <code><head></code> 中的标签渲染到正确位置——JSX 只渲染到 <code>root</code> 节点</li> <li>社区库（react-helmet / react-helmet-async）使用 React 的 <code>context</code> + 副作用（<code><Helmet></code> 组件在挂载时更新 <code>document.title</code> 和 DOM head）</li> <li>react-helmet 已归档不再维护，react-helmet-async 依赖 <code>HelmetProvider</code> 包裹</li> </ul> <p><strong>自动合并规则</strong>：</p> <ol> <li><strong>同名标签</strong>：最深层（子组件）的标签优先级最高（覆盖父组件）</li> <li><strong>同属性标签</strong>：<code><meta name="description"></code> 会按 name 属性去重，深层覆盖浅层</li> <li><strong>多个不同标签共存</strong>：如 <code><link rel="stylesheet"></code> 和 <code><meta charset="utf-8"></code> 同时存在</li> </ol> <p><strong>SSR 支持</strong>：服务端渲染时自动将 <code><title></code>/<code><meta></code> 注入到 <code><head></code>，客户端 hydration 后无缝接管。</p> <p><strong>React 19 的实现原理</strong>：</p> <ol> <li>React 在渲染时识别 <code><title></code>、<code><meta></code>、<code><link></code> 等 head 标签</li> <li>将它们从组件树中”提取”出来，渲染到 <code><head></code> 中</li> <li>支持服务端渲染——SSR 时直接写出到 HTML head</li> <li><strong>去重</strong>：多个组件渲染同名的 meta 标签时，以后渲染的为准（属于”last wins”策略）</li> </ol> <p><strong>深入思考</strong>：</p> <ul> <li><strong>react-helmet 为什么不需要了</strong>：React 19 原生支持 Document Metadata，第三方库（react-helmet、react-helmet-async）的绝大多数用例已被原生 API 覆盖。只有特殊需求（如 SSR 中复杂的 head 管理、动态 meta 标签注入）才需要继续使用</li> <li><strong>Server Components 中可直接使用</strong>：由于 Server Component 不需要 <code>useEffect</code>，在 RSC 中设置 <code><title></code> 比 React 18 的 <code>useEffect</code> 方案更自然、更高效</li> <li><strong>生产踩坑</strong>：如果同时使用 react-helmet 和 React 19 原生 metadata，会出现 title 重复或冲突。迁移时需确保只使用一套方案</li> <li><strong>SSR 差异</strong>：React 19 的 Document Metadata 在服务端渲染时直接在 HTML 中输出到 <code><head></code>，不会出现闪动（FOUC）</li> <li><strong>动态更新</strong>：SPA 中导航时，<code><title></code> 会自动更新为当前页面组件的值，不需要手动调 <code>document.title = ...</code></li> <li><strong>不支持 <code><script></code></strong>：<code><script></code> 标签不会自动提升到 head。需要用 <code><Helmet></code> 或 <code><Script></code> 组件（next/script）</li> </ul> <p>参考：<a href="https://react.dev/blog/2024/12/05/react-19#support-for-metadata-tags">React 19 - Document Metadata</a></p> <figure class="highlight plaintext"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line">---</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line">### 15. React 生产性能分析与调优：React DevTools Profiler、Chrome Performance 和关键指标</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line">**标准答案**：</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line">React 应用性能问题常见于「不必要的重渲染」和「组件挂载/卸载抖动」。生产环境下的性能分析需要系统性的方法。</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line">**关键性能指标**：</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line">| 指标 | 含义 | 理想值 | 测量方式 |</span><br><span class="line">|------|------|-------|---------|</span><br><span class="line">| **FCP** (First Contentful Paint) | 首屏内容渲染时间 | < 1.5s | Lighthouse / Web Vitals |</span><br><span class="line">| **LCP** (Largest Contentful Paint) | 最大内容渲染时间 | < 2.5s | Web Vitals |</span><br><span class="line">| **INP** (Interaction to Next Paint) | 交互响应时间 | < 200ms | Web Vitals（2024 年替代 FID） |</span><br><span class="line">| **Render Time** | 组件渲染耗时 | < 16ms (60fps) | React DevTools Profiler |</span><br><span class="line">| **Commit Count** | 不必要的重渲染次数 | 0（交互后无多余提交） | React DevTools |</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line">**性能分析三板斧**：</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line">**1. React DevTools Profiler —— 组件级性能分析**</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line">```tsx</span><br><span class="line">// 用 Profiler 组件包裹目标区域</span><br><span class="line">import { Profiler } from 'react';</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line">function onRenderCallback(</span><br><span class="line"> id: string,</span><br><span class="line"> phase: 'mount' | 'update' | 'nested-update',</span><br><span class="line"> actualDuration: number,</span><br><span class="line"> baseDuration: number,</span><br><span class="line"> startTime: number,</span><br><span class="line"> commitTime: number,</span><br><span class="line"> interactions: Set<any></span><br><span class="line">) {</span><br><span class="line"> // 记录到性能监控系统</span><br><span class="line"> performanceMonitor.record(id, { actualDuration, phase, commitTime });</span><br><span class="line">}</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line">function App() {</span><br><span class="line"> return (</span><br><span class="line"> <Profiler id="Sidebar" onRender={onRenderCallback}></span><br><span class="line"> <Sidebar /></span><br><span class="line"> </Profiler></span><br><span class="line"> );</span><br><span class="line">}</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>2. Chrome Performance Tab —— 宏观性能分析</strong></p> <p>录制交互 → 查看 <strong>Main</strong> → 筛选 <strong>Timing</strong> → 定位 <code>React</code> 相关任务</p> <ul> <li><strong>黄色长任务</strong>（> 50ms）→ 可能阻塞主线程 → 检查是否可以用 <code>useDeferredValue</code> 或 <code>startTransition</code></li> <li><strong>Layout 抖動</strong> → 查看 Force Reflow → 检查组件的样式读写模式</li> <li><strong>网络瀑布图</strong> → 检查 API 调用顺序：是否有串行请求本该并行？</li> </ul> <p><strong>3. 生产监控 —— 真实用户性能</strong></p> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br><span class="line">12</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 使用 Web Vitals API 收集真实用户数据</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">import</span> { onCLS, onFCP, onLCP, onINP } <span class="keyword">from</span> <span class="string">'web-vitals'</span>;</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">sendToAnalytics</span>(<span class="params"><span class="attr">metric</span>: <span class="built_in">any</span></span>) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> body = <span class="title function_">onCLS</span>(sendToAnalytics);</span><br><span class="line"><span class="title function_">onFCP</span>(sendToAnalytics);</span><br><span class="line"><span class="title function_">onLCP</span>(sendToAnalytics);</span><br><span class="line"><span class="title function_">onINP</span>(sendToAnalytics);</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>常见性能问题的定位与解法</strong>：</p> <table> <thead> <tr> <th>问题表象</th> <th>根因</th> <th>解法</th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr> <td>列表滚动卡顿</td> <td>每行组件重渲染过多</td> <td>使用 <code>React.memo</code> + <code>useMemo</code> + <code>key</code> 稳定化</td> </tr> <tr> <td>表单项输入延迟</td> <td>输入事件触发全表单重渲染</td> <td>将输入项拆为独立子组件 + <code>React.memo</code>；或用 React Compiler</td> </tr> <tr> <td>页面切换白屏</td> <td>组件初次挂载时大量同步计算</td> <td>使用 <code>lazy()</code> + Suspense 代码分割；数据用 <code>use()</code> 流式加载</td> </tr> <tr> <td>弹窗/模态框打开卡顿</td> <td>弹窗内容包含大量计算或 DOM</td> <td>使用 <code><Activity mode="hidden"></code>（React 19.2）预渲染并保持状态</td> </tr> </tbody></table> <p><strong>深入思考</strong>：</p> <ul> <li><strong>React Compiler + React DevTools 的组合</strong>：2025 年最佳实践——先用 React Compiler（自动 memo），再通过 Profiler 检查 Compiler 未能优化的边界情况（如复杂计算、大型列表），手动优化剩余瓶颈</li> <li><strong>INP 取代 FID 的意义</strong>：FID 只测量首次交互延迟，而 INP 测量所有交互的延迟（取最差 p75 值）。这迫使团队关注每次点击/键盘操作的响应性，而不仅仅是首屏</li> <li><strong>避免过早优化</strong>：在用户反馈卡顿之前，专注于代码质量和架构设计。React Compiler 已能处理 80% 的 memo 需求</li> </ul> <p>参考：<a href="https://web.dev/vitals/">Web Vitals</a>、<a href="https://react.dev/learn/react-developer-tools">React DevTools Profiler</a></p> <p><strong>面试金句</strong>：「先测量，再优化」是 React 性能优化的第一原则。不要猜瓶颈在哪里——Chrome Performance Tab 和 React Profiler 会告诉你。猜出来的「优化」大半是安慰剂。</p> <hr> <h3 id="16-React-与-Web-Components-互操作：在-React-19-中使用-Web-Components-的最佳实践"><a href="#16-React-与-Web-Components-互操作：在-React-19-中使用-Web-Components-的最佳实践" class="headerlink" title="16. React 与 Web Components 互操作：在 React 19 中使用 Web Components 的最佳实践"></a>16. React 与 Web Components 互操作：在 React 19 中使用 Web Components 的最佳实践</h3><p><strong>标准答案</strong>：</p> <p>Web Components（Custom Elements + Shadow DOM）是浏览器原生组件标准。React 19 大幅改善了对 Web Components 的支持。</p> <p><strong>React 19 的核心改进</strong>：</p> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span 的问题</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// - 事件需要手动 addEventListener（因为 Custom Events 不遵循 React 的合成事件）</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// - class 必须转 className（Web Components 期望 class）</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// - 复杂属性需要 JSON.stringify</span></span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span <span class="title function_">useEffect</span>(<span class="function">() =></span> {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> el = ref.<span 手动绑定</span></span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">return</span> <span class="function">() =></span> el.<span class="title function_">removeEventListener</span>(<span /></span></span>;</span><br><span class="line">}</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="name">MyWidget</span>></span></span></span><br><span class="line"> );</span><br><span class="line">}</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>React 19 的局限</strong>：</p> <table> <thead> <tr> <th>功能</th> <th>React 18</th> <th>React 19</th> <th>备注</th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr> <td>className → class</td> <td>❌ 需手动</td> <td>✅ 自动转换</td> <td>重大改进</td> </tr> <tr> <td>对象/数组 props</td> <td>❌ 需 JSON.stringify</td> <td>✅ 自动 setProperty</td> <td>重大改进</td> </tr> <tr> <td>Custom Events</td> <td>❌ 需 addEventListener</td> <td>✅ onMyEvent 绑定</td> <td>重大改进</td> </tr> <tr> <td>Form 关联表单元素</td> <td>❌ 不兼容</td> <td>❌ 仍不兼容</td> <td><code><form></code> 中 <code><input></code> 等内建元素才支持</td> </tr> <tr> <td>表单验证 API</td> <td>❌ 不兼容</td> <td>❌ 仍不兼容</td> <td><code>setCustomValidity()</code> 等 API 不在 React 合成事件处理</td> </tr> <tr> <td>子元素内容分发</td> <td>✅ slot 支持</td> <td>✅ slot 支持</td> <td>一直可用</td> </tr> </tbody></table> <p><strong>深入思考</strong>：</p> <ul> <li><strong>微前端中的 Web Components</strong>：在微前端架构中，不同框架（React/Vue/Angular）的子应用可以通过 Web Components 相互暴露 UI 组件——React 19 的改进让这一模式更加无缝</li> <li><strong>React 19 中为什么之前不支持</strong>：过去 Web Components 和 React 的 Prop 传递机制冲突（React 对所有 props 做字符串化，而 WC 需要 setProperty），React 19 在 Reconciliation 层做了特殊处理</li> <li><strong>生产踩坑</strong>：Web Components 的样式通常封装在 Shadow DOM 中，React 应用的全局 CSS 无法穿透。需要 WC 开发者提供 CSS Custom Properties（CSS 变量）作为样式接口</li> </ul> <p>参考：<a href="https://react.dev/blog/2024/12/05/react-19#support-for-web-components-with-custom-elements">React 19 - Web Components</a></p> <hr> <h2 id="0x04-React-19-新特性与生产实践"><a href="#0x04-React-19-新特性与生产实践" class="headerlink" title="0x04 React 19 新特性与生产实践"></a>0x04 React 19 新特性与生产实践</h2><h3 id="22-React-19-use-Hook-深度解析——在渲染中直接消费-Promise"><a href="#22-React-19-use-Hook-深度解析——在渲染中直接消费-Promise" class="headerlink" title="22. React 19 use() Hook 深度解析——在渲染中直接消费 Promise"></a>22. React 19 <code>use()</code> Hook 深度解析——在渲染中直接消费 Promise</h3><p><strong>难度</strong>：⭐⭐⭐⭐（专家）</p> <p><strong>问题</strong>：React 19 引入的 <code>use()</code> Hook 允许在渲染过程中直接消费 Promise，它如何改变了 React 的异步数据处理模式？</p> <p><strong>核心原理</strong>：</p> <figure class="highlight typescript"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="string">'react'</span>;</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// use() 可以在渲染时直接读取 Promise 的值</span></span><br><span class="line"><span <span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><<span class="name">div</span>></span>{order.name} - {order.status}<span class="tag"></<span class="name">div</span>></span></span>;</span><br><span <th><code>use()</code> + Suspense（React 19）</th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr> <td>代码行数</td> <td>~15 行（loading/success/error）</td> <td>~5 行</td> </tr> <tr> <td>渲染次数</td> <td>3 次（mount → loading → data）</td> <td>2 次（fallback → data）</td> </tr> <tr> <td>竞态条件</td> <td>需手动取消 <code>AbortController</code></td> <td>自动处理</td> </tr> <tr> <td>错误处理</td> <td><code>try/catch in useEffect</code></td> <td><code><ErrorBoundary></code></td> </tr> <tr> <td>SSR 支持</td> <td>需手动处理</td> <td>原生支持</td> </tr> <tr> <td>状态管理</td> <td>需 useReducer/第三方</td> <td>React 内置</td> </tr> </tbody></table> <p><strong>🔥 踩坑案例：Server Action + <code>use()</code> 在 Client Component 中的错误用法（某电商团队）</strong></p> <ul> <li><strong>场景</strong>：使用 React 19 Server Actions + <code>use()</code> 实现表单查询</li> <li><strong>问题</strong>：在 Client Component 中直接调用 Server Action 时，<code>use()</code> 报错</li> </ul> <figure class="highlight typescript"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span );</span><br><span class="line">}</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">OrderResult</span>(<span re-fetch</span></span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> order = <span class="title function_">use</span>(promise);</span><br><span class="line"> <span Server Components only），需要包裹在 <code><Suspense></code> 中并配合 Server Component 使用</li> </ul> <p><strong>面试金句</strong>：</p> <blockquote> <p>“React 19 的 <code>use()</code> 把数据获取从 <code>useEffect</code> 的世界拉到声明式渲染中。不必再手动管理 loading/error/竞态。但记住——<code>use()</code> 在 Server Components 中完全稳定，在 Client Components 中仍是实验性功能。”</p> </blockquote> <p><strong>参考</strong>：</p> <ul> <li><a href="https://react.dev/reference/react/use">React 19 use() documentation</a></li> <li><a href="https://dev.to/a1guy/react-19-use-hook-deep-dive-using-promises-directly-in-your-components-1plp">DEV Community: React 19 use() Deep Dive</a></li> </ul> <h3 id="23-React-Server-Components-在-2026-年的生产最佳实践"><a href="#23-React-Server-Components-在-2026-年的生产最佳实践" class="headerlink" title="23. React Server Components 在 2026 年的生产最佳实践"></a>23. React Server Components 在 2026 年的生产最佳实践</h3><p><strong>难度</strong>：⭐⭐⭐⭐（专家）</p> <p><strong>问题</strong>：React Server Components（RSC）经历了 2 年多的生产验证，2026 年有哪些经过验证的最佳实践和踩坑？</p> <p><strong>核心原理</strong>：</p> <figure class="highlight plaintext"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br><span class="line">12</span><br><span class="line">13</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line">graph TD</span><br><span class="line"> subgraph "Server"</span><br><span class="line"> RSC[Server Component<br/>只在服务端运行] --> DB[(数据库)]</span><br><span class="line"> RSC --> FS[文件系统]</span><br><span class="line"> RSC --> API[内部 API]</span><br><span class="line"> RSC --> R[渲染为 RSC Payload]</span><br><span class="line"> end</span><br><span class="line"> </span><br><span class="line"> subgraph "Client"</span><br><span class="line"> R --> CC[Client Component<br/>保持交互性]</span><br><span class="line"> CC --> State[useState/useEffect]</span><br><span class="line"> CC --> UserEvent[用户事件]</span><br><span class="line"> end</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>2026 年 RSC 生产最佳实践</strong>：</p> <figure class="highlight typescript"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br><span class="line">12</span><br><span class="line">13</span><br><span class="line">14</span><br><span class="line">15</span><br><span class="line">16</span><br><span class="line">17</span><br><span class="line">18</span><br><span class="line">19</span><br><span class="line">20</span><br><span class="line">21</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 1. 数据获取层 → 只在 Server Component 中</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// app/orders/page.tsx</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">import</span> { db } <span class="keyword">from</span> <span class="string">'@/lib/db'</span>;</span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">import</span> { <span class="title class_">OrderCard</span> } <span class="keyword">from</span> <span class="string">'./OrderCard'</span>; <span class="comment">// Client Component</span></span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">async</span> <span <figure class="highlight typescript"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span Client Component 最小化原则</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="string">'use client'</span>;</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// ✅ 只在需要交互时才用 class="line">}</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>🔥 踩坑案例：Client Component 意外包裹 Server Component 导致水合失败（某 SaaS 公司）</strong></p> <ul> <li><strong>场景</strong>：使用 Next.js App Router 重构报表页面</li> <li><strong>症状</strong>：页面刷新后 UI 闪烁（先显示正确的报表，然后消失显示 loading）</li> <li><strong>排查</strong>：<ol> <li>发现 <code>Chart.js</code> 的封装组件用了 <code>'use client'</code></li> <li>但这个 Client Component 的内部又 import 了一个 Server Component 用于数据加载</li> <li>React 18/19 不允许 Client Component 的子组件是 Server Component</li> </ol> </li> <li><strong>根因</strong>：Client Component 的 <code>children</code> 可以是 Server Component（通过 <code>server component as children</code> 模式），但直接 import 不行</li> <li><strong>修复</strong>：</li> </ul> <figure class="highlight typescript"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br><span class="line">12</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line"><span class="comment">// ✅ 正确：Client Component 通过 children 接收 Server Component</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// app/reports/page.tsx</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">import</span> { <span class="title class_">ChartClient</span> } <span class="keyword">from</span> <span class="string">'./ChartClient'</span>; <span class="comment">// 'use client'</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">import</span> { <span class="title class_">ChartData</span> } <span class="keyword">from</span> <span class="string">'./ChartData'</span>; <span class="comment">// Server Component</span></span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">export</span> <span class="keyword">default</span> <span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">ReportsPage</span>(<span class="params"></span>) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">return</span> (</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><<span class="name">ChartClient</span>></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"><<span class="name">ChartData</span> /></span> {/* Server Component 作为 children 传入 */}</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"></<span class="name">ChartClient</span>></span></span></span><br><span class="line"> );</span><br><span class="line">}</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>RSC 生产 Checklist</strong>：</p> <table> <thead> <tr> <th>检查项</th> <th>说明</th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr> <td><code>'use client'</code> 尽量下沉</td> <td>只有需要 <code>useState/useEffect/onClick</code> 的组件才标 client</td> </tr> <tr> <td>Server Component 不直接 import Client Component</td> <td>通过 children/Props 传递</td> </tr> <tr> <td>所有数据获取在 Server Component 中</td> <td>避免”客户端→API→数据库”的多余跳转</td> </tr> <tr> <td>RSC Payload 大小监控</td> <td>大的 Server Component 树会产生大 Payload</td> </tr> <tr> <td>Hooks 不可在 Server Component 使用</td> <td>Server Component 必须是 async function</td> </tr> </tbody></table> <p><strong>面试金句</strong>：</p> <blockquote> <p>“React Server Components 的生产最佳实践可以总结为一句话：Server 负责数据，Client 负责交互。<code>'use client'</code> 关键字用在你需要 <code>useState/useEffect/onClick</code> 的地方，否则默认都是 Server Component。最大的坑是 Client Component 不能直接 Import Server Component——要用 <code>children</code> 传递。”</p> </blockquote> <p><strong>参考</strong>：</p> <ul> <li><a href="https://www.growin.com/blog/react-server-components">Growin: React Server Components in Production 2026</a></li> <li><a href="https://react.dev/reference/rsc/server-components">React Server Components 官方文档</a></li> </ul> <hr> <h3 id="31-React-Server-Components-生产模式：数据获取、缓存与-Suspense-边界设计"><a href="#31-React-Server-Components-生产模式：数据获取、缓存与-Suspense-边界设计" class="headerlink" title="31. React Server Components 生产模式：数据获取、缓存与 Suspense 边界设计"></a>31. React Server Components 生产模式：数据获取、缓存与 Suspense 边界设计</h3><p><strong>难度</strong>：⭐⭐⭐（高级）<br><strong>问题</strong>：RSC 改变了数据获取的心智模型。请设计一套生产级 RSC 的数据获取模式，包含缓存策略、Suspense 边界和错误处理。</p> <p><strong>核心原理</strong>：</p> <p>RSC 的数据获取模式不同于传统 SPA：</p> <figure class="highlight plaintext"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line">传统 SPA（客户端获取）:</span><br><span class="line"> 渲染 → useEffect → loading → 客户端 fetch → 渲染</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line">RSC（服务端获取）:</span><br><span class="line"> 服务端直接 await db.query() → 渲染 HTML + 流式传输 → 客户端显示</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>三种数据获取模式对比</strong>：</p> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br><span class="line">12</span><br><span class="line">13</span><br><span class="line">14</span><br><span class="line">15</span><br><span class="line">16</span><br><span class="line">17</span><br><span class="line">18</span><br><span class="line">19</span><br><span class="line">20</span><br><span class="line">21</span><br><span class="line">22</span><br><span class="line">23</span><br><span class="line">24</span><br><span class="line">25</span><br><span class="line">26</span><br><span class="line">27</span><br><span class="line">28</span><br><span class="line">29</span><br><span class="line">30</span><br><span class="line">31</span><br><span class="line">32</span><br><span class="line">33</span><br><span class="line">34</span><br><span class="line">35</span><br><span class="line">36</span><br><span class="line">37</span><br><span class="line">38</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 模式 1：直接服务端获取（推荐）</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 优点：零客户端请求，最快速</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 缺点：页面级加载，没有细粒度 loading</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">async</span> <span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">UserPage</span>(<span class="params">{ userId }: { userId: <span class="built_in">string</span> }</span>) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> user = <span class="keyword">await</span> db.<span class="property">users</span>.<span class="title function_">findById</span>(userId); <span class="comment">// 直接在组件中 await</span></span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">return</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><<span class="name">div</span>></span>{user.name}<span 包裹（推荐）</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 优点：流式传输，逐块渲染</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 缺点：需要合理设计 Suspense 边界</span></span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">async</span> <span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">UserProfile</span>(<span class="params">{ userId }: { userId: <span class="built_in">string</span> }</span>) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> user = <span class="keyword">await</span> db.<span class="property">users</span>.<span class="title function_">findById</span>(userId);</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">return</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">Page</span>(<span class="params">{ params }: { params: { id: <span class="built_in">string</span> } }</span>) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">return</span> (</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><<span class="string">{</span><<span class="attr">ProfileSkeleton</span> /></span>}></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"><<span class="name">UserProfile</span> <span class="attr">userId</span>=<span class="string">{params.id}</span> /></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"></<span );</span><br><span class="line">}</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 模式 3：客户端再获取（仅用于需要客户端状态的场景）</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="string">'use client'</span>;</span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">LiveData</span>(<span class="params"></span>) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> { data } = <span class="title function_">useSWR</span>(<span class="string">'/api/live'</span>, fetcher, { <span class="attr">refreshInterval</span>: <span class="number">5000</span> });</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">return</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><<span class="name">div</span>></span>{data.value}<span class="tag"></<span class="name">div</span>></span></span>;</span><br><span class="line">}</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>Suspense 边界设计原则</strong>：</p> <figure class="highlight plaintext"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br><span class="line">12</span><br><span class="line">13</span><br><span class="line">14</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line">Suspense 边界粒度:</span><br><span class="line"> 页级 Suspense → 加载慢（等待全部数据）</span><br><span class="line"> 组件级 Suspense → 用户体验好（逐块展示）</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line">推荐粒度：按照"视觉区域"划分</span><br><span class="line"> ┌─────────────────────────────┐</span><br><span class="line"> │ <Suspense> 头部导航 │ ← 静态，不需要 Suspense</span><br><span class="line"> ├─────────────────────────────┤</span><br><span class="line"> │ <Suspense> 主内容区 │ ← 主要数据等待</span><br><span class="line"> │ ├── <Suspense> 用户信息 │ ← 快速查询</span><br><span class="line"> │ └── <Suspense> 订单列表 │ ← 慢查询</span><br><span class="line"> ├─────────────────────────────┤</span><br><span class="line"> │ <Suspense> 推荐侧边栏 │ ← 优先级最低</span><br><span class="line"> └─────────────────────────────┘</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>RSC 缓存策略</strong>：</p> <figure class="highlight plaintext"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line">Next.js 中的 RSC 缓存：</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line">静态（Static）：无动态数据 → 构建时生成 → 最快</span><br><span class="line">动态（Dynamic）：有动态数据 → 请求时生成 → 实时</span><br><span class="line">增量（ISR）：混合策略 → 按需重新验证 → 平衡</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line">配置示例：</span><br><span class="line">// app/page.tsx</span><br><span class="line">export const dynamic = 'force-dynamic'; // 强制动态</span><br><span class="line">// 或使用 revalidate：</span><br><span class="line">export const revalidate = 3600; // 每小时重新验证</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>生产踩坑案例</strong>：</p> <p><strong>🔥 案例：RSC Suspense 瀑布导致加载时长翻倍（某电商平台，2025）</strong></p> <ul> <li><strong>场景</strong>：商品详情页使用 RSC + Suspense，10 个数据组件</li> <li><strong>症状</strong>：页面完全加载耗时从 1.2s 增加到 4.5s</li> <li><strong>排查</strong>：检查 Network 瀑布图发现 Suspense 边界嵌套过深</li> <li><strong>根因</strong>：<code><ProductPage></code> → <code><Suspense></code> → <code><Details></code> → <code><Suspense></code> → <code><Price></code> → 每个 Suspense 串行等待</li> <li><strong>修复</strong>：将非依赖的数据获取提升到同一层级，并行加载</li> <li><strong>效果</strong>：加载时间恢复至 1.5s</li> </ul> <p><strong>面试金句</strong>：</p> <blockquote> <p>RSC 最大的心智模型转变是：<strong>数据获取从客户端事件的响应（useEffect）变成了服务端组件树的声明（async component）</strong>。但这也带来了新的挑战——Suspense 边界设计得不好，RSC 的优势（流式传输）反而会退化成串行瀑布。</p> </blockquote> <hr> <h3 id="32-React-19-useOptimistic-和-useActionState-模式：乐观更新与表单状态管理"><a href="#32-React-19-useOptimistic-和-useActionState-模式：乐观更新与表单状态管理" class="headerlink" title="32. React 19 useOptimistic 和 useActionState 模式：乐观更新与表单状态管理"></a>32. React 19 useOptimistic 和 useActionState 模式：乐观更新与表单状态管理</h3><p><strong>难度</strong>：⭐⭐⭐（高级）<br><strong>问题</strong>：React 19 引入了 useOptimistic 和 useActionState。请说明如何在生产中使用这些 API 实现良好的用户体验。</p> <p><strong>核心原理</strong>：</p> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br><span class="line">12</span><br><span class="line">13</span><br><span class="line">14</span><br><span class="line">15</span><br><span class="line">16</span><br><span class="line">17</span><br><span class="line">18</span><br><span class="line">19</span><br><span class="line">20</span><br><span class="line">21</span><br><span class="line">22</span><br><span class="line">23</span><br><span class="line">24</span><br><span class="line">25</span><br><span class="line">26</span><br><span class="line">27</span><br><span class="line">28</span><br><span class="line">29</span><br><span class="line">30</span><br><span class="line">31</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line"><span class="string">'use client'</span>;</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">import</span> { useOptimistic, useActionState, useRef } <span class="keyword">from</span> <span class="string">'react'</span>;</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// useOptimistic：乐观更新</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">MessageList</span>(<span class="params">{ messages, sendMessage }</span>) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> [optimisticMessages, addOptimisticMessage] = <span class="title function_">useOptimistic</span>(</span><br><span class="line"> messages,</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="function">(<span class="params">state, newMessage</span>) =></span> [...state, { <span class="attr">id</span>: <span class="string">'pending'</span>, ...newMessage, <span class="attr">sending</span>: <span class="literal">true</span> }]</span><br><span class="line"> );</span><br><span class="line"> </span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">return</span> (</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><<span class="name">div</span>></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> {optimisticMessages.map(msg => (</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"><<span class="name">div</span> <span class="attr">key</span>=<span class="string">{msg.id}</span> <span class="attr">className</span>=<span class="string">{msg.sending</span> ? '<span class="attr">opacity-50</span>' <span class="attr">:</span> ''}></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> {msg.text}</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"></<span class="name">div</span>></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"></<span class="name">form</span>></span></span></span><br><span class="line">);</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line">---</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line">### <span class="number">16.</span> <span class="title class_">React</span> <span class="number">19</span> 升级踩坑——资深研发必须知道的风险清单</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line">**标准答案**：</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line">从 <span class="title class_">React</span> <span class="number">18</span> 升级到 <span class="number">19</span>，很多<span class="string">"静默"</span>的变化可能在线上出问题。以下是资深研发在升级时需要重点排查的清单：</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line">**<span class="number">1.</span> <span class="string">`forwardRef`</span> 废弃警告**</span><br><span class="line"><span class="string">``</span><span class="string">`txt</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="string">Warning: forwardRef is deprecated and will be removed in a future major release.</span></span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <ul> <li>解决：改为在函数组件中直接接收 <code>ref</code> prop</li> <li>注意：第三方库（如 Radix UI、react-hook-form）可能还没全部迁移，检查依赖后再升级</li> </ul> <p><strong>2. 废弃的 <code>propTypes</code> 和 <code>defaultProps</code> 在函数组件中不再工作</strong></p> <ul> <li><code>propTypes</code> 对函数组件完全无效（Class 组件仍然可用）</li> <li><code>defaultProps</code> 对函数组件不再生效——必须用 ES6 默认参数</li> </ul> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line"><span class="comment">// ❌ 不再工作</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">Button</span>(<span class="params">{ label }</span>) { ... }</span><br><span class="line"><span class="title class_">Button</span>.<span class="property">defaultProps</span> = { <span class="attr">label</span>: <span class="string">'Click'</span> };</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// ✅ 使用 ES6 默认值</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">Button</span>(<span class="params">{ label = <span class="string">'Click'</span> }</span>) { ... }</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>3. <code>ReactDOM.render</code> 完全移除</strong></p> <ul> <li><code>ReactDOM.render(<App />, container)</code> → 必须用 <code>createRoot</code></li> <li>老项目如果还在用 <code>ReactDOM.render</code> 会直接报错</li> </ul> <p><strong>4. <code>useMemo</code>、<code>useCallback</code> 在 StrictMode 中行为变化</strong></p> <ul> <li>React 19 的 StrictMode 在开发模式下重新渲染时，会复用首次渲染的 <code>useMemo</code>/<code>useCallback</code> 结果</li> <li>这可能导致某些依赖”副作用”的逻辑出现不一致</li> </ul> <p><strong>5. 不同 React 版本共存导致 Hook 规则错误</strong></p> <ul> <li>如果同时使用了 React 18 和 19（如 npm 依赖嵌套），会报 <code>Invalid hook call</code>——检查 <code>node_modules</code> 中是否有多份 React</li> </ul> <p><strong>6. TypeScript 类型变更</strong></p> <ul> <li><code>@types/react@19</code> 移除了 <code>React.FC</code> 的 <code>children</code> 隐式声明（需要显式声明 <code>children?: React.ReactNode</code>）</li> <li><code>React.Ref</code> 类型的声明方式变化</li> </ul> <p><strong>7. 测试库兼容性</strong></p> <ul> <li><code>@testing-library/react</code> 需要更新到 v16+ 才能兼容 React 19</li> <li><code>react-test-renderer</code> 已弃用，建议迁移到 <code>@testing-library/react</code></li> </ul> <p><strong>升级 checklist 推荐</strong>：</p> <figure class="highlight txt"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line">□ 先升到 React 18.3（获取所有废弃警告）</span><br><span class="line">□ 运行 codemod：npx codemod@latest react/19/migration-recipe</span><br><span class="line">□ 检查第三方库的 React 19 兼容性（npm outdated）</span><br><span class="line">□ 检查 propTypes/defaultProps 使用</span><br><span class="line">□ 检查 ReactDOM.render 调用</span><br><span class="line">□ 检查 forwardRef 使用</span><br><span class="line">□ 更新 TypeScript 类型包</span><br><span class="line">□ 更新测试库</span><br><span class="line">□ 全面回归测试</span><br><span class="line">□ 逐步灰度上线</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p>参考：<a href="https://react.dev/blog/2024/04/25/react-19-upgrade-guide">React 19 Upgrade Guide</a></p> <hr> <h2 id="0x08-Server-Components（RSC）深度原理"><a href="#0x08-Server-Components（RSC）深度原理" class="headerlink" title="0x08 Server Components（RSC）深度原理"></a>0x08 Server Components（RSC）深度原理</h2><h3 id="17-RSC-的架构原理是什么？Streaming-HTML-和-Server-Actions-是怎么协同的？"><a href="#17-RSC-的架构原理是什么？Streaming-HTML-和-Server-Actions-是怎么协同的？" class="headerlink" title="17. RSC 的架构原理是什么？Streaming HTML 和 Server Actions 是怎么协同的？"></a>17. RSC 的架构原理是什么？Streaming HTML 和 Server Actions 是怎么协同的？</h3><p><strong>标准答案</strong>：</p> <p>RSC 架构的核心是一个<strong>双向数据流</strong>系统：</p> <figure class="highlight plaintext"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br><span class="line">12</span><br><span class="line">13</span><br><span class="line">14</span><br><span class="line">15</span><br><span class="line">16</span><br><span class="line">17</span><br><span class="line">18</span><br><span class="line">19</span><br><span class="line">20</span><br><span class="line">21</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line">客户端浏览器 服务端</span><br><span class="line"> │ │</span><br><span class="line"> ├── 首次请求 ──────────────────────► │</span><br><span class="line"> │ │ Server Component 渲染</span><br><span class="line"> │ │ → 直接查询 DB/FS</span><br><span class="line"> │ │ → 生成 RSC Payload（序列化 Virtual DOM）</span><br><span class="line"> │ │</span><br><span class="line"> │◄── Stream RSC Payload + HTML ────── │</span><br><span class="line"> │ (分块发送，Suspense 边界可独立流) │</span><br><span class="line"> │ │</span><br><span class="line"> │ React 客户端重建 VDOM │</span><br><span class="line"> │ 水合交互部分 │</span><br><span class="line"> │ │</span><br><span class="line"> ├── 用户点击/表单提交 ─────────────► │</span><br><span class="line"> │ (Server Action via POST) │</span><br><span class="line"> │ │ 执行 Server Action</span><br><span class="line"> │ │ → 更新数据库</span><br><span class="line"> │ │ → revalidatePath()</span><br><span class="line"> │ │</span><br><span class="line"> │◄── 新的 RSC Payload ─────────────── │</span><br><span class="line"> │ (无需全量刷新，仅更新变化部分) │</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>关键概念</strong>：</p> <p><strong>1. RSC Payload</strong>：不是 HTML，而是序列化的 React 元素树——一个 JSON 数组，包含组件类型、props 和引用：</p> <figure class="highlight js"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line"><span class="comment">// RSC Payload 简化结构</span></span><br><span class="line">[</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="string">"$"</span>, <span class="comment">// 标记为 React 元素</span></span><br><span class="line"> <span class="string">"div"</span>, <span class="comment">// 元素类型</span></span><br><span class="line"> <span class="literal">null</span>, <span class="comment">// key</span></span><br><span class="line"> { <span class="attr">className</span>: <span class="string">"container"</span> }, <span class="comment">// props</span></span><br><span class="line"> [</span><br><span class="line"> [<span class="string">"$"</span>, <span class="string">"h1"</span>, <span class="literal">null</span>, { <span class="attr">children</span>: <span class="string">"Hello World"</span> }],</span><br><span class="line"> [<span class="string">"$"</span>, <span class="string">"@1"</span>, <span class="literal">null</span>, {}], <span class="comment">// "@1" 引用 Client Component 模块 ID</span></span><br><span class="line"> ]</span><br><span class="line">]</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>2. Streaming</strong>：Server Component 可以按 Suspense 边界分段流式传输：</p> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line"><span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">Page</span>(<span class="params"></span>) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">return</span> (</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><<span class="name">Layout</span>></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"><<span class="name">Nav</span> /></span> {/* 立即发出 */}</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"><<span class="name">Suspense</span> <span class="attr">fallback</span>=<span class="string">{</span><<span class="attr">Loading</span> /></span>}></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"><<span class="name">SlowData</span> /></span> {/* 数据准备好后再流式传输 */}</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"></<span class="name">Suspense</span>></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"></<span class="name">Layout</span>></span></span></span><br><span class="line"> );</span><br><span class="line">}</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>3. Server Actions 的协作流程</strong>：</p> <ul> <li>表单提交 → 浏览器 POST 到服务端 Action 端点</li> <li>服务端执行 Action（带 Cookie、Session）</li> <li>执行完成后调用 <code>revalidatePath()</code> 或 <code>revalidateTag()</code></li> <li>服务端重新渲染受影响的 Server Component</li> <li>新增 RSC Payload 推送回客户端，React 原地更新 DOM</li> </ul> <p><strong>面试金句</strong>：RSC 的本质不是”服务端渲染”，而是”服务端渲染组件树并序列化为客户端可以消费的协议格式”。Server Actions 提供了从客户端触发服务端数据变更的能力，两者结合构成了”后端驱动前端”的全栈范式。</p> <p>参考：<a href="https://react.dev/reference/rsc/server-components">RSC 官方文档</a></p> <hr> <h3 id="18-Server-Component-vs-Client-Component-的分界策略是什么？"><a href="#18-Server-Component-vs-Client-Component-的分界策略是什么？" class="headerlink" title="18. Server Component vs Client Component 的分界策略是什么？"></a>18. Server Component vs Client Component 的分界策略是什么？</h3><p><strong>标准答案</strong>：</p> <p>决定一个组件应该是 Server 还是 Client，遵循以下决策树：</p> <figure class="highlight txt"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line">组件是否需要以下功能？</span><br><span class="line">├── useState / useReducer / useRef → 是 → 🟢 Client Component</span><br><span class="line">├── useEffect / 生命周期 → 是 → 🟢 Client Component</span><br><span class="line">├── onClick / onChange / 事件处理 → 是 → 🟢 Client Component</span><br><span class="line">├── 浏览器 API（window/document/localStorage）→ 是 → 🟢 Client Component</span><br><span class="line">├── 自定义 Hook（内部用了以上 API）→ 是 → 🟢 Client Component</span><br><span class="line">├── 纯展示、数据获取、格式化 → 否 → 🔵 Server Component</span><br><span class="line">└── "不太确定"</span><br><span class="line"> ├── 能挪到 Server 就尽量 Server → 🔵 Server Component</span><br><span class="line"> └── 实在不行加 'use client' → 🟢 Client Component</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>实战分界技巧</strong>：</p> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br><span class="line">12</span><br><span class="line">13</span><br><span class="line">14</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line"><span class="comment">// ✅ 推荐：页面层是 Server Component（负责数据获取+布局）</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">async</span> <span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">UserProfilePage</span>(<span class="params">{ userId }: { userId: <span class="built_in">string</span> }</span>) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> user = <span class="keyword">await</span> db.<span class="property">user</span>.<span class="title function_">findUnique</span>({ <span class="attr">where</span>: { <span class="attr">id</span>: userId } });</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">return</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><<span class="name">UserProfileCard</span> <span class="attr">user</span>=<span class="string">{user}</span> /></span></span>;</span><br><span class="line">}</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// ✅ 把交互部分"隔离"到小的 Client Component</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="string">'use client'</span>;</span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">FollowButton</span>(<span class="params">{ userId }: { userId: <span class="built_in">string</span> }</span>) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> [followed, setFollowed] = <span class="title function_">useState</span>(<span class="literal">false</span>);</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">return</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><<span class="name">button</span> <span class="attr">onClick</span>=<span class="string">{()</span> =></span> setFollowed(!followed)}></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> {followed ? '已关注' : '关注'}</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"></<span class="name">button</span>></span></span>;</span><br><span class="line">}</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>模式：Server Component 包裹 Client Component</strong></p> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">19</span><br><span class="line">20</span><br><span class="line">21</span><br><span class="line">22</span><br><span class="line">23</span><br><span class="line">24</span><br><span class="line">25</span><br><span class="line">26</span><br><span class="line">27</span><br><span class="line">28</span><br><span class="line">29</span><br><span class="line">30</span><br><span class="code"><pre><span class="line"><span class="comment">// Server Component</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">async</span> <span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">ProductList</span>(<span class="params"></span>) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> products = <span class="keyword">await</span> <span useActionState（原 useFormState）：表单状态绑定</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">AddToCartForm</span>(<span class="params">{ productId
