<span class="attr">message</span>: e.<span class="property">message</span> };</span><br><span class="line"> }</span><br><span class="line"> },</span><br><span class="line"> { <span class="attr">success</span>: <span class="literal">false</span>, <span class="attr">message</span>: <span class="string">''</span> }</span><br><span class="line"> );</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">return</span> (</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><<span class="name">form</span> <span class="attr">action</span>=<span class="string">{formAction}</span>></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"><<span class="name">input</span> <span class="attr">type</span>=<span class="string">"number"</span> <span class="attr">name</span>=<span class="string">"quantity"</span> <span class="attr">defaultValue</span>=<span class="string">{1}</span> /></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"><<span class="name">button</span> <span class="attr">type</span>=<span class="string">"submit"</span> <span class="attr">disabled</span>=<span class="string">{isPending}</span>></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> {isPending ? '添加中...' : '加入购物车'}</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"></<span class="name">button</span>></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> {state.message && (</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"><<span class="name">p</span> <span class="attr">className</span>=<span class="string">{state.success</span> ? '<span class="attr">text-green-500</span>' <span class="attr">:</span> '<span class="attr">text-red-500</span>'}></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> {state.message}</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"></<span class="name">p</span>></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> )}</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"></<span class="name">form</span>></span></span></span><br><span class="line"> );</span><br><span class="line">}</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>深入思考</strong>：</p> <ul> <li><strong>Server Component 不能直接 import Client Component 作为子组件？</strong> 能！Server Component 可以 import 和渲染 Client Component，但 Client Component 不能 import Server Component</li> <li><strong>‘use client’ 的传染性</strong>：一旦标记 <code>'use client'</code>，该文件及其所有子组件都变成 Client Component（除非子组件也是用 <code>'use server'</code> 标记的独立函数）</li> <li><strong>最佳实践</strong>：尽量让 Server Component 做”重活”（数据获取 + 布局），Client Component 做”轻活”（交互 + 状态）</li> </ul> <p>参考：<a href="https://react.dev/reference/rsc/use-client">RSC 分界指南</a></p> <hr> <h3 id="19-RSC-与传统-SSR-的核心区别是什么？为什么说-RSC-不是-SSR-的替代？"><a href="#19-RSC-与传统-SSR-的核心区别是什么？为什么说-RSC-不是-SSR-的替代？" class="headerlink" title="19. RSC 与传统 SSR 的核心区别是什么？为什么说 RSC 不是 SSR 的替代？"></a>19. RSC 与传统 SSR 的核心区别是什么？为什么说 RSC 不是 SSR 的替代？</h3><p><strong>标准答案</strong>：</p> <table> <thead> <tr> <th>维度</th> <th>传统 SSR (React 18-)</th> <th>RSC (React 19+)</th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr> <td><strong>输出格式</strong></td> <td>HTML 字符串</td> <td>RSC Payload（序列化 VDOM）+ HTML 流</td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>组件是否发送到客户端</strong></td> <td>所有组件的 JS bundle 都发送</td> <td>Server Component 的 JS <strong>零发送</strong></td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>数据获取方式</strong></td> <td><code>getServerSideProps</code> 或手动注水</td> <td>组件内部直接 <code>async/await</code> 或 <code>use()</code></td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>交互性（水合）</strong></td> <td>必须水合整个页面</td> <td>只需水合 Client Component 部分</td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>流式传输</strong></td> <td>可选的（<code>renderToPipeableStream</code>）</td> <td><strong>默认</strong>流式，按 Suspense 边界</td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>缓存粒度</strong></td> <td>页面级（ISR）</td> <td>组件级 + 数据级</td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>状态保持</strong></td> <td>页面间导航丢失滚动/输入状态</td> <td>RSC Payload 保持 Client 状态</td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>适用场景</strong></td> <td>内容型网站，需要完整 HTML</td> <td>混合型应用，部分交互+部分服务端</td> </tr> </tbody></table> <p><strong>为什么 RSC 不是替代 SSR 的？</strong></p> <p>RSC 和 SSR 解决不同维度的问题：</p> <ul> <li><strong>SSR（Server-Side Rendering）</strong>：解决的是”首屏怎么更快”——把 JS 生成 HTML，让用户更早看到内容</li> <li><strong>RSC（React Server Components）</strong>：解决的是”哪些代码不需要发到客户端”——让服务端组件不贡献 JS bundle 大小</li> </ul> <figure class="highlight txt"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line">最理想的架构：RSC + SSR Streaming（Next.js App Router）</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line">首屏请求 → SSR Streaming 快速输出 HTML 骨架</span><br><span class="line"> ↓</span><br><span class="line"> 逐步流式发送 RSC Payload（各 Suspense 边界独立）</span><br><span class="line"> ↓</span><br><span class="line"> 客户端用 RSC Payload 重建 VDOM + 水合 Client Component</span><br><span class="line"> ↓</span><br><span class="line"> 后续导航 → 仅请求 RSC Payload（无需全量 HTML）</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>深入思考</strong>：</p> <ul> <li><strong>Bundle 节省</strong>：一个 Server Component 若用 moment.js 做日期格式化，传统 SSR 会把 moment.js 整个发送到客户端；RSC 下 moment.js 只存在于服务端</li> <li><strong>交互性差距</strong>：传统 SSR 必须等待完整水合才能交互；RSC + Streaming 让可交互部分（Client Components）优先水合</li> </ul> <p>参考：<a href="https://www.developerway.com/posts/react-server-components-performance">RSC vs SSR 深度解析</a></p> <hr> <h3 id="20-RSC-的序列化限制是什么？哪些东西不能从-Server-Component-传到-Client-Component？"><a href="#20-RSC-的序列化限制是什么？哪些东西不能从-Server-Component-传到-Client-Component？" class="headerlink" title="20. RSC 的序列化限制是什么？哪些东西不能从 Server Component 传到 Client Component？"></a>20. RSC 的序列化限制是什么？哪些东西不能从 Server Component 传到 Client Component？</h3><p><strong>标准答案</strong>：</p> <p>Server Component 渲染的结果会序列化为 RSC Payload（JSON-like 格式）发往客户端，因此<strong>只有可序列化的值才能作为 Server Component 的 props 传递给 Client Component</strong>：</p> <p><strong>不能传递的类型</strong>：</p> <table> <thead> <tr> <th>类型</th> <th>原因</th> <th>示例</th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr> <td><strong>函数</strong></td> <td>JSON 无法表示函数</td> <td><code>function() {}</code>、<code>() => {}</code>、方法</td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>Date 对象</strong></td> <td>序列化为字符串而非 Date</td> <td><code>new Date()</code> → 客户端拿到的是字符串</td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>Class 实例</strong></td> <td>原型链丢失</td> <td><code>new MyClass()</code></td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>Map / Set</strong></td> <td>非 JSON 原生类型</td> <td><code>new Map()</code>、<code>new Set()</code></td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>Symbol</strong></td> <td>JSON 不支持</td> <td><code>Symbol('id')</code></td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>undefined</strong></td> <td>JSON.stringify 会移除</td> <td>通常变为缺失字段</td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>循环引用对象</strong></td> <td>JSON.stringify 会报错</td> <td><code>const a = {}; a.self = a;</code></td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>React Element</strong></td> <td>除非用 <code>cloneElement</code> 特殊处理</td> <td><code><div /></code> 不能直接传递</td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>Request/Response</strong></td> <td>浏览器 API，不可序列化</td> <td>只在 HTTP 层有效</td> </tr> </tbody></table> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br><span class="line">12</span><br><span class="line">13</span><br><span class="line">14</span><br><span class="line">15</span><br><span class="line">16</span><br><span class="line">17</span><br><span class="line">18</span><br><span class="line">19</span><br><span class="line">20</span><br><span class="line">21</span><br><span class="line">22</span><br><span class="line">23</span><br><span class="line">24</span><br><span class="line">25</span><br><span class="line">26</span><br><span class="line">27</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line"><span class="comment">// ❌ 错误：传递不可序列化的值</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">ServerComponent</span>(<span class="params"></span>) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> date = <span class="keyword">new</span> <span class="title class_">Date</span>();</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> <span class="title function_">handler</span> = (<span class="params"></span>) => <span class="variable language_">console</span>.<span class="title function_">log</span>(<span class="string">'click'</span>);</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> map = <span class="keyword">new</span> <span class="title class_">Map</span>([[<span class="string">'key'</span>, <span class="string">'value'</span>]]);</span><br><span class="line"> </span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">return</span> (</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><<span class="name">ClientComponent</span></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="tag"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="attr">date</span>=<span class="string">{date}</span> // ❌ <span class="attr">客户端拿到的是字符串</span> "<span class="attr">2026-06-13T...</span>"</span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="tag"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="attr">onClick</span>=<span class="string">{handler}</span> // ❌ <span class="attr">函数无法序列化</span></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="tag"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="attr">data</span>=<span class="string">{map}</span> // ❌ <span class="attr">Map</span> <span class="attr">无法序列化</span></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="tag"><span class="language-xml"> /></span></span></span><br><span class="line"> );</span><br><span class="line">}</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// ✅ 正确：提前转换</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">ServerComponent</span>(<span class="params"></span>) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> timestamp = <span class="title class_">Date</span>.<span class="title function_">now</span>(); <span class="comment">// number 可序列化</span></span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> items = [{ <span class="attr">id</span>: <span class="number">1</span>, <span class="attr">name</span>: <span class="string">'a'</span> }]; <span class="comment">// 普通 JSON 对象</span></span><br><span class="line"> </span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">return</span> (</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><<span class="name">ClientComponent</span></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="tag"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="attr">timestamp</span>=<span class="string">{timestamp}</span></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="tag"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="attr">items</span>=<span class="string">{items}</span></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="tag"><span class="language-xml"> /></span></span></span><br><span class="line"> );</span><br><span class="line">}</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>特殊处理技巧</strong>：</p> <ul> <li><strong>Date 对象</strong>：传 <code>date.toISOString()</code>，在 Client Component 中 <code>new Date(isoString)</code></li> <li><strong>需要回调的场景</strong>：Server Component 不能传递 onclick 给 Client Component——交互必须封装在 Client Component 内部</li> <li><strong>类实例</strong>：拆解为普通对象传输，Client 侧重新实例化</li> </ul> <p><strong>面试金句</strong>：RSC 的序列化限制本质上是”服务端和客户端之间的网络边界”。一旦你接受了这个限制，模式就很清晰了——Server 负责数据准备，Client 负责交互行为。</p> <p>参考：<a href="https://react.dev/reference/rsc/server-components#serializable-types">RSC 序列化规则</a></p> <hr> <h3 id="21-Server-Actions-的安全注意事项——资深研发必知"><a href="#21-Server-Actions-的安全注意事项——资深研发必知" class="headerlink" title="21. Server Actions 的安全注意事项——资深研发必知"></a>21. Server Actions 的安全注意事项——资深研发必知</h3><p><strong>标准答案</strong>：</p> <p>每个 <code>'use server'</code> 函数本质上是一个<strong>公开的 HTTP POST 端点</strong>——不论你写多少 TypeScript 类型和前端校验，攻击者可以用 <code>curl</code> 直接调用。必须把 Server Action 当作 API 来防护：</p> <p><strong>五大安全陷阱</strong>：</p> <p><strong>1. 输入校验缺失</strong></p> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br><span class="line">12</span><br><span class="line">13</span><br><span class="line">14</span><br><span class="line">15</span><br><span class="line">16</span><br><span class="line">17</span><br><span class="line">18</span><br><span class="line">19</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line"><span class="comment">// ❌ 危险：依赖 TypeScript 类型——运行时不存在</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="string">'use server'</span>;</span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">export</span> <span class="keyword">async</span> <span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">deleteUser</span>(<span class="params"><span class="attr">userId</span>: <span class="built_in">string</span></span>) { <span class="comment">// 任何人可以传任何值</span></span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">await</span> db.<span class="property">user</span>.<span class="title function_">delete</span>({ <span class="attr">where</span>: { <span class="attr">id</span>: userId } });</span><br><span class="line">}</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// ✅ 安全：运行时校验</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="string">'use server'</span>;</span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">import</span> { z } <span class="keyword">from</span> <span class="string">'zod'</span>;</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">const</span> <span class="title class_">DeleteUserSchema</span> = z.<span class="title function_">object</span>({</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="attr">userId</span>: z.<span class="title function_">string</span>().<span class="title function_">uuid</span>(),</span><br><span class="line">});</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">export</span> <span class="keyword">async</span> <span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">deleteUser</span>(<span class="params"><span class="attr">input</span>: <span class="title class_">FormData</span></span>) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> raw = <span class="title class_">Object</span>.<span class="title function_">fromEntries</span>(input);</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> { userId } = <span class="title class_">DeleteUserSchema</span>.<span class="title function_">parse</span>(raw);</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">await</span> db.<span class="property">user</span>.<span class="title function_">delete</span>({ <span class="attr">where</span>: { <span class="attr">id</span>: userId } });</span><br><span class="line">}</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>2. 认证检查缺失</strong></p> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line"><span class="comment">// ❌ 危险：任何知道 userId 的人都可以操作</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="string">'use server'</span>;</span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">export</span> <span class="keyword">async</span> <span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">deleteUser</span>(<span class="params"><span class="attr">userId</span>: <span class="built_in">string</span></span>) { ... }</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// ✅ 安全：每个 Action 校验会话</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="string">'use server'</span>;</span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">export</span> <span class="keyword">async</span> <span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">deleteUser</span>(<span class="params"></span>) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> session = <span class="keyword">await</span> <span class="title function_">getSession</span>();</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">if</span> (!session?.<span class="property">user</span>) <span class="keyword">throw</span> <span class="keyword">new</span> <span class="title class_">Error</span>(<span class="string">'Unauthorized'</span>);</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="comment">// ...</span></span><br><span class="line">}</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>3. 授权（Authorization）遗漏</strong></p> <ul> <li>认证 ≠ 授权——用户已登录不代表他能删除别人的数据</li> </ul> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line"><span class="comment">// ✅ 在数据库查询中嵌入用户 ID</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">await</span> db.<span class="property">task</span>.<span class="title function_">deleteMany</span>({</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="attr">where</span>: { <span class="attr">id</span>: taskId, <span class="attr">ownerId</span>: session.<span class="property">user</span>.<span class="property">id</span> },</span><br><span class="line">});</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>4. CSRF 误解</strong></p> <ul> <li>Next.js Server Actions <strong>有内置的 Origin 头校验</strong>，提供基础的 CSRF 防护</li> <li>但 API Routes 没有！如果 Server Action 调用了内部的 API Route，需要额外防护</li> </ul> <p><strong>5. 速率限制缺失</strong></p> <ul> <li>Server Action 可被无限调用 → 可能造成 DoS 或高额账单</li> </ul> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br><span class="line">12</span><br><span class="line">13</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line"><span class="keyword">import</span> { <span class="title class_">Ratelimit</span> } <span class="keyword">from</span> <span class="string">'@upstash/ratelimit'</span>;</span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">import</span> { headers } <span class="keyword">from</span> <span class="string">'next/headers'</span>;</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">const</span> ratelimit = <span class="keyword">new</span> <span class="title class_">Ratelimit</span>({</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="attr">limiter</span>: <span class="title class_">Ratelimit</span>.<span class="title function_">slidingWindow</span>(<span class="number">5</span>, <span class="string">'1m'</span>),</span><br><span class="line">});</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">export</span> <span class="keyword">async</span> <span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">resetPassword</span>(<span class="params"><span class="attr">input</span>: <span class="title class_">FormData</span></span>) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> ip = (<span class="keyword">await</span> <span class="title function_">headers</span>()).<span class="title function_">get</span>(<span class="string">'x-forwarded-for'</span>) ?? <span class="string">'unknown'</span>;</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> { success } = <span class="keyword">await</span> ratelimit.<span class="title function_">limit</span>(ip);</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">if</span> (!success) <span class="keyword">return</span> { <span class="attr">error</span>: <span class="string">'Too many requests'</span> };</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="comment">// ...</span></span><br><span class="line">}</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>面试金句</strong>：Server Actions 的便利性是一把双刃剑——它消除了 API 层的样板代码，但也意味着你需要在前端代码中嵌入服务端安全逻辑。规则很简单：<strong>对每一个 <code>'use server'</code> 函数，问自己——如果这是一个公开的 POST 端点，我该怎么做安全防护？</strong></p> <p>参考：<a href="https://makerkit.dev/blog/tutorials/secure-nextjs-server-actions">Secure Next.js Server Actions</a></p> <hr> <h2 id="0x09-Next-js-App-Router-生产实战"><a href="#0x09-Next-js-App-Router-生产实战" class="headerlink" title="0x09 Next.js App Router 生产实战"></a>0x09 Next.js App Router 生产实战</h2><h3 id="22-App-Router-vs-Pages-Router-的选型建议？"><a href="#22-App-Router-vs-Pages-Router-的选型建议？" class="headerlink" title="22. App Router vs Pages Router 的选型建议？"></a>22. App Router vs Pages Router 的选型建议？</h3><p><strong>标准答案</strong>：</p> <table> <thead> <tr> <th>维度</th> <th>Pages Router</th> <th>App Router</th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr> <td><strong>路由定义</strong></td> <td>文件即路由（<code>pages/about.tsx</code>）</td> <td>文件即路由 + 路由组/平行路由/拦截路由</td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>数据获取</strong></td> <td><code>getServerSideProps</code> / <code>getStaticProps</code></td> <td>组件内 <code>async/await</code> + <code>fetch()</code></td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>组件模型</strong></td> <td>所有组件都是 Client Component</td> <td>默认 Server Component，<code>'use client'</code> 标记</td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>Layout</strong></td> <td>需自定义 <code>_app.tsx</code> + 手动嵌套</td> <td>内置 Layout 系统（<code>layout.tsx</code>）</td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>Loading</strong></td> <td>无内置支持</td> <td>内置 <code>loading.tsx</code>（Suspense-based）</td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>Streaming</strong></td> <td>14.0+ 通过 <code>renderToPipeableStream</code> 手动</td> <td>默认基于 Suspense 流式</td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>Server Actions</strong></td> <td>不支持</td> <td>原生支持</td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>ISR / SSG</strong></td> <td>支持（<code>getStaticPaths</code>）</td> <td>支持（<code>generateStaticParams</code> + <code>revalidate</code>）</td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>SEO</strong></td> <td>手动管理</td> <td>内置 Document Metadata</td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>中间件</strong></td> <td>支持（<code>_middleware.ts</code>）</td> <td>支持（<code>middleware.ts</code>，更灵活）</td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>成熟度</strong></td> <td>非常成熟，生态丰富</td> <td>持续完善中，部分高级模式仍需探索</td> </tr> </tbody></table> <p><strong>选型建议</strong>：</p> <figure class="highlight txt"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br><span class="line">12</span><br><span class="line">13</span><br><span class="line">14</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line">✅ 新项目 → App Router（首选）</span><br><span class="line"> ├── 需要 RSC 减 bundle 大小</span><br><span class="line"> ├── 需要 Streaming 提升首屏性能</span><br><span class="line"> ├── 需要 Server Actions 简化数据变更</span><br><span class="line"> └── 需要 Layout/Loading/Error 内置路由能力</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line">✅ 老项目迁移 → 评估成本</span><br><span class="line"> ├── 简单内容型 → App Router 迁移成本低</span><br><span class="line"> ├── 复杂交互型 → 混合模式过渡（App + Pages）</span><br><span class="line"> └── 重度依赖第三方 Hub → 确认兼容性后再迁移</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line">⚠️ 暂不迁移</span><br><span class="line"> ├── 维护成本 > 收益的小项目</span><br><span class="line"> └── 大量使用 custom server（App Router 更依赖 Vercel 平台）</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>面试金句</strong>：Vercel 官方已明确 Pages Router 不会有新功能，所有新特性（RSC、Server Actions、Streaming）都在 App Router 上。Pages Router 会继续维护但已是”维护模式”。</p> <p>参考：<a href="https://nextjs.org/docs/app/building-your-application/routing">Next.js Routing Comparison</a></p> <hr> <h3 id="23-路由组（Route-Groups）、平行路由（Parallel-Routes）、拦截路由（Intercepting-Routes）分别解决什么问题？"><a href="#23-路由组（Route-Groups）、平行路由（Parallel-Routes）、拦截路由（Intercepting-Routes）分别解决什么问题？" class="headerlink" title="23. 路由组（Route Groups）、平行路由（Parallel Routes）、拦截路由（Intercepting Routes）分别解决什么问题？"></a>23. 路由组（Route Groups）、平行路由（Parallel Routes）、拦截路由（Intercepting Routes）分别解决什么问题？</h3><p><strong>标准答案</strong>：</p> <p><strong>1. 路由组 (Route Groups)</strong> — <code>(groupName)</code></p> <p>解决<strong>不需要在 URL 中体现的组织需求</strong>，比如同一个路径下需要多个 layout：</p> <figure class="highlight txt"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line">app/</span><br><span class="line">├── (marketing)/ ← URL 无前缀</span><br><span class="line">│ ├── layout.tsx ← 营销页面的 layout</span><br><span class="line">│ ├── page.tsx → /</span><br><span class="line">│ └── about/page.tsx → /about</span><br><span class="line">├── (shop)/</span><br><span class="line">│ ├── layout.tsx ← 商城页面的 layout</span><br><span class="line">│ ├── products/page.tsx → /products</span><br><span class="line">│ └── cart/page.tsx → /cart</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p>常见的生产场景：A/B 测试不同 layout、按团队/模块拆分而不影响 URL。</p> <p><strong>2. 平行路由 (Parallel Routes)</strong> — <code>@slotName</code></p> <p>解决<strong>同一页面中多个独立区域同时渲染</strong>的问题：</p> <figure class="highlight txt"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line">app/</span><br><span class="line">├── dashboard/</span><br><span class="line">│ ├── @analytics/page.tsx ← URL: /dashboard, 区域: analytics</span><br><span class="line">│ ├── @notifications/page.tsx ← URL: /dashboard, 区域: notifications</span><br><span class="line">│ ├── default.tsx</span><br><span class="line">│ └── page.tsx ← URL: /dashboard, 区域: children</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br><span class="line">12</span><br><span class="line">13</span><br><span class="line">14</span><br><span class="line">15</span><br><span class="line">16</span><br><span class="line">17</span><br><span class="line">18</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line"><span class="comment">// app/dashboard/layout.tsx</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">export</span> <span class="keyword">default</span> <span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">DashboardLayout</span>(<span class="params">{</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="params"> children, // 隐式 slot</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="params"> analytics, // @analytics 对应的 slot</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="params"> notifications, // @notifications 对应的 slot</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="params">}: {</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="params"> children: React.ReactNode;</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="params"> analytics: React.ReactNode;</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="params"> notifications: React.ReactNode;</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="params">}</span>) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">return</span> (</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><<span class="name">div</span> <span class="attr">className</span>=<span class="string">"grid grid-cols-3"</span>></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"><<span class="name">main</span>></span>{children}<span class="tag"></<span class="name">main</span>></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"><<span class="name">aside</span>></span>{analytics}<span class="tag"></<span class="name">aside</span>></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"><<span class="name">aside</span>></span>{notifications}<span class="tag"></<span class="name">aside</span>></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"></<span class="name">div</span>></span></span></span><br><span class="line"> );</span><br><span class="line">}</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>3. 拦截路由 (Intercepting Routes)</strong> — <code>(.)</code> / <code>(..)</code> / <code>(...)</code> </p> <p>解决<strong>从当前页面导航到某个路由时，在模态框中显示而不是页面跳转</strong>的问题：</p> <figure class="highlight txt"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line">app/</span><br><span class="line">├── feed/</span><br><span class="line">│ └── page.tsx → /feed</span><br><span class="line">├── photo/</span><br><span class="line">│ └── [id]/</span><br><span class="line">│ └── page.tsx → /photo/1（直接访问：完整页面）</span><br><span class="line">└── @modal/</span><br><span class="line"> └── (.)photo/</span><br><span class="line"> └── [id]/</span><br><span class="line"> └── page.tsx → 从 feed 中点开：模态框</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <ul> <li><code>(.)</code> — 同级拦截</li> <li><code>(..)</code> — 上一级拦截</li> <li><code>(...)</code> — 根级拦截</li> <li><code>(..)(..)</code> — 上两级拦截</li> </ul> <p><strong>生产案例：Instagram 的照片浏览器</strong></p> <figure class="highlight txt"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line">从 /feed 点击照片 → 模态框显示（平行路由 + 拦截路由）</span><br><span class="line">直接访问 /photo/123 → 完整页面显示</span><br><span class="line">刷新时模态框内容 → 自动 fallback 到默认页面</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>面试金句</strong>：平行路由 + 拦截路由是 Modal + Deep Linking 的”必杀技”——直接访问时是完整页面，导航访问时是模态框，URL 始终保持唯一可分享。这是传统 React Router 很难完美实现的模式。</p> <p>参考：<a href="https://nextjs.org/docs/app/building-your-application/routing/parallel-routes">Next.js Parallel Routes</a></p> <hr> <h3 id="24-App-Router-数据获取策略：fetch-cache-revalidate-的最佳实践"><a href="#24-App-Router-数据获取策略：fetch-cache-revalidate-的最佳实践" class="headerlink" title="24. App Router 数据获取策略：fetch + cache + revalidate 的最佳实践"></a>24. App Router 数据获取策略：fetch + cache + revalidate 的最佳实践</h3><p><strong>标准答案</strong>：</p> <p>Next.js App Router 扩展了原生 <code>fetch()</code> API，添加了 <code>cache</code> 和 <code>next.revalidate</code> 选项：</p> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br><span class="line">12</span><br><span class="line">13</span><br><span class="line">14</span><br><span class="line">15</span><br><span class="line">16</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 三种核心策略</span></span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 1. 静态数据（类似 SSG）— 构建时获取，永不重新验证</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">const</span> data = <span class="keyword">await</span> <span class="title function_">fetch</span>(<span class="string">'https://api.example.com/data'</span>, {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="attr">cache</span>: <span class="string">'force-cache'</span>, <span class="comment">// 默认行为</span></span><br><span class="line">});</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 2. 动态数据（类似 SSR）— 每次请求都重新获取</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">const</span> data = <span class="keyword">await</span> <span class="title function_">fetch</span>(<span class="string">'https://api.example.com/data'</span>, {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="attr">cache</span>: <span class="string">'no-store'</span>, <span class="comment">// 或 next: { revalidate: 0 }</span></span><br><span class="line">});</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 3. ISR — 缓存到指定时间后重新验证</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">const</span> data = <span class="keyword">await</span> <span class="title function_">fetch</span>(<span class="string">'https://api.example.com/data'</span>, {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="attr">next</span>: { <span class="attr">revalidate</span>: <span class="number">60</span> }, <span class="comment">// 60 秒后重新验证</span></span><br><span class="line">});</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>细粒度缓存失效 (Tag-based Revalidation)</strong>：</p> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br><span class="line">12</span><br><span class="line">13</span><br><span class="line">14</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 在 fetch 时打标签</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">const</span> data = <span class="keyword">await</span> <span class="title function_">fetch</span>(<span class="string">'https://api.example.com/posts'</span>, {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="attr">next</span>: { <span class="attr">tags</span>: [<span class="string">'posts'</span>] },</span><br><span class="line">});</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 在 Server Action 中按标签失效</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="string">'use server'</span>;</span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">export</span> <span class="keyword">async</span> <span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">createPost</span>(<span class="params"></span>) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">await</span> db.<span class="property">post</span>.<span class="title function_">create</span>({ ... });</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="title function_">revalidateTag</span>(<span class="string">'posts'</span>); <span class="comment">// 所有 tags 包含 'posts' 的缓存失效</span></span><br><span class="line">}</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 或按路径失效</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="title function_">revalidatePath</span>(<span class="string">'/posts'</span>); <span class="comment">// /posts 路径下的所有缓存失效</span></span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>决策树</strong>：</p> <figure class="highlight txt"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line">数据是否需要实时？</span><br><span class="line">├── 否 → cache: 'force-cache'（静态资源、配置数据）</span><br><span class="line">├── 部分实时 → next: { revalidate: N }（文章列表、评论数）</span><br><span class="line">└── 是 → cache: 'no-store'（用户信息、购物车、实时数据）</span><br><span class="line"> ├── 还可以用动态函数：cookies()、headers() 自动 opt-out 缓存</span><br><span class="line"> └── 或者用 unstable_noStore() 声明不缓存</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>生产最佳实践</strong>：</p> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br><span class="line">12</span><br><span class="line">13</span><br><span class="line">14</span><br><span class="line">15</span><br><span class="line">16</span><br><span class="line">17</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line"><span class="comment">// ✅ 推荐：每个 fetch 明确指定缓存策略</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">async</span> <span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">DashboardPage</span>(<span class="params"></span>) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="comment">// 数据 A：用户基本信息（实时）</span></span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> user = <span class="keyword">await</span> <span class="title function_">fetch</span>(<span class="string">'/api/user'</span>, { <span class="attr">cache</span>: <span class="string">'no-store'</span> });</span><br><span class="line"> </span><br><span class="line"> <span class="comment">// 数据 B：统计数据（每分钟更新）</span></span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> stats = <span class="keyword">await</span> <span class="title function_">fetch</span>(<span class="string">'/api/stats'</span>, { </span><br><span class="line"> <span class="attr">next</span>: { <span class="attr">revalidate</span>: <span class="number">60</span>, <span class="attr">tags</span>: [<span class="string">'dashboard-stats'</span>] } </span><br><span class="line"> });</span><br><span class="line"> </span><br><span class="line"> <span class="comment">// 数据 C：侧边栏菜单（几乎不变）</span></span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> menu = <span class="keyword">await</span> <span class="title function_">fetch</span>(<span class="string">'/api/menu'</span>, { <span class="attr">cache</span>: <span class="string">'force-cache'</span> });</span><br><span class="line"> </span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">return</span> (</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><<span class="name">Dashboard</span> <span class="attr">user</span>=<span class="string">{user}</span> <span class="attr">stats</span>=<span class="string">{stats}</span> <span class="attr">menu</span>=<span class="string">{menu}</span> /></span></span></span><br><span class="line"> );</span><br><span class="line">}</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>面试金句</strong>：App Router 的数据获取核心变化是”去中心化”——不再有 <code>getServerSideProps</code> 这样的顶层数据方法，数据获取分散到每个组件中，配合 cache 语义实现按需更新。这意味着你需要对每个 fetch 显式声明缓存意图。</p> <p>参考：<a href="https://nextjs.org/docs/app/building-your-application/data-fetching">Next.js Data Fetching</a></p> <hr> <h3 id="25-ISR-SSG-SSR-Streaming-的选择决策树"><a href="#25-ISR-SSG-SSR-Streaming-的选择决策树" class="headerlink" title="25. ISR / SSG / SSR / Streaming 的选择决策树"></a>25. ISR / SSG / SSR / Streaming 的选择决策树</h3><p><strong>标准答案</strong>：</p> <figure class="highlight txt"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br><span class="line">12</span><br><span class="line">13</span><br><span class="line">14</span><br><span class="line">15</span><br><span class="line">16</span><br><span class="line">17</span><br><span class="line">18</span><br><span class="line">19</span><br><span class="line">20</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line">页面内容是否需要实时？</span><br><span class="line">├── 完全不需要 → SSG (Static Site Generation)</span><br><span class="line">│ ├── 构建时生成 HTML</span><br><span class="line">│ ├── 最快、成本最低、CDN 友好</span><br><span class="line">│ └── 适合：博客文章、文档、营销首页</span><br><span class="line">│</span><br><span class="line">├── 需要定期更新 → ISR (Incremental Static Regeneration)</span><br><span class="line">│ ├── 构建时生成 + 按时间自动更新</span><br><span class="line">│ ├── 平衡：缓存命中率与新鲜度</span><br><span class="line">│ └── 适合：新闻列表、商品目录、排行榜</span><br><span class="line">│</span><br><span class="line">├── 每次请求都更新内容 → SSR (Server-Side Rendering)</span><br><span class="line">│ ├── 每次请求重新渲染 HTML</span><br><span class="line">│ ├── 最新数据，但延迟较高</span><br><span class="line">│ └── 适合：用户仪表盘、搜索页面、社交信息流</span><br><span class="line">│</span><br><span class="line">└── 需要快的首屏但部分数据慢 → Streaming</span><br><span class="line"> ├── 分块发送 HTML，先展示骨架</span><br><span class="line"> ├── 改善感知性能（LCP 更低）</span><br><span class="line"> └── 适合：混合页面（快数据+慢数据并存）</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>实际生产中的组合模式</strong>：</p> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br><span class="line">12</span><br><span class="line">13</span><br><span class="line">14</span><br><span class="line">15</span><br><span class="line">16</span><br><span class="line">17</span><br><span class="line">18</span><br><span class="line">19</span><br><span class="line">20</span><br><span class="line">21</span><br><span class="line">22</span><br><span class="line">23</span><br><span class="line">24</span><br><span class="line">25</span><br><span class="line">26</span><br><span class="line">27</span><br><span class="line">28</span><br><span class="line">29</span><br><span class="line">30</span><br><span class="line">31</span><br><span class="line">32</span><br><span class="line">33</span><br><span class="line">34</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 页面级：SSR + Streaming（Next.js App Router 默认行为）</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">async</span> <span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">DashboardPage</span>(<span class="params"></span>) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">return</span> (</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><<span class="name">PageLayout</span>></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> {/* 这部分立即流式输出 */}</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"><<span class="name">Header</span> <span class="attr">user</span>=<span class="string">{await</span> <span class="attr">getFastUser</span>()} /></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> </span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> {/* 这部分等待数据，但不会阻塞整个页面 */}</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"><<span class="name">Suspense</span> <span class="attr">fallback</span>=<span class="string">{</span><<span class="attr">ChartSkeleton</span> /></span>}></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"><<span class="name">SlowChart</span> /></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"></<span class="name">Suspense</span>></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> </span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> {/* 不同数据源独立流式 */}</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"><<span class="name">Suspense</span> <span class="attr">fallback</span>=<span class="string">{</span><<span class="attr">ListSkeleton</span> /></span>}></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"><<span class="name">SlowRecommendations</span> /></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"></<span class="name">Suspense</span>></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"></<span class="name">PageLayout</span>></span></span></span><br><span class="line"> );</span><br><span class="line">}</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 组件级：混用 ISR 和动态数据（通过 fetch cache 策略）</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">async</span> <span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">ProductPage</span>(<span class="params">{ params }: { params: { id: <span class="built_in">string</span> } }</span>) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="comment">// 产品信息：ISR（60 秒）</span></span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> product = <span class="keyword">await</span> <span class="title function_">fetch</span>(<span class="string">`/api/products/<span class="subst">${params.id}</span>`</span>, {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="attr">next</span>: { <span class="attr">revalidate</span>: <span class="number">60</span> },</span><br><span class="line"> });</span><br><span class="line"> </span><br><span class="line"> <span class="comment">// 库存信息：实时</span></span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> stock = <span class="keyword">await</span> <span class="title function_">fetch</span>(<span class="string">`/api/stock/<span class="subst">${params.id}</span>`</span>, {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="attr">cache</span>: <span class="string">'no-store'</span>,</span><br><span class="line"> });</span><br><span class="line"> </span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">return</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><<span class="name">ProductDetail</span> <span class="attr">product</span>=<span class="string">{product}</span> <span class="attr">stock</span>=<span class="string">{stock}</span> /></span></span>;</span><br><span class="line">}</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>深入思考</strong>：</p> <ul> <li><strong>重新验证成本</strong>：ISR 不是免费的——每次 revalidate 都会触发服务端渲染。如果页面访问量极大，ISR 的突发渲染请求可能压垮数据库</li> <li><strong>Streaming 的 SEO 影响</strong>：Google 支持渲染流式内容，但复杂的 Streaming 模式可能导致爬虫无法完整抓取。关键 SEO 页面建议使用 SSG 或 SSR（非 Streaming）</li> <li><strong>混合策略</strong>：生产中最常见的模式是”外层 ISR，内层 Streaming”——页面整体每 60s 更新，但内部的用户专属模块实时渲染</li> </ul> <p>参考：<a href="https://nextjs.org/docs/app/building-your-application/rendering">Next.js Rendering Strategies</a></p> <hr> <h3 id="26-Next-js-中间件（Middleware）的生产使用"><a href="#26-Next-js-中间件（Middleware）的生产使用" class="headerlink" title="26. Next.js 中间件（Middleware）的生产使用"></a>26. Next.js 中间件（Middleware）的生产使用</h3><p><strong>标准答案</strong>：</p> <p>Next.js Middleware 在<strong>边缘</strong>（Edge Runtime）执行，在路由匹配之前拦截请求：</p> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br><span class="line">12</span><br><span class="line">13</span><br><span class="line">14</span><br><span class="line">15</span><br><span class="line">16</span><br><span class="line">17</span><br><span class="line">18</span><br><span class="line">19</span><br><span class="line">20</span><br><span class="line">21</span><br><span class="line">22</span><br><span class="line">23</span><br><span class="line">24</span><br><span class="line">25</span><br><span class="line">26</span><br><span class="line">27</span><br><span class="line">28</span><br><span class="line">29</span><br><span class="line">30</span><br><span class="line">31</span><br><span class="line">32</span><br><span class="line">33</span><br><span class="line">34</span><br><span class="line">35</span><br><span class="line">36</span><br><span class="line">37</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line"><span class="comment">// middleware.ts（项目根目录）</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">import</span> { <span class="title class_">NextResponse</span> } <span class="keyword">from</span> <span class="string">'next/server'</span>;</span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">import</span> <span class="keyword">type</span> { <span class="title class_">NextRequest</span> } <span class="keyword">from</span> <span class="string">'next/server'</span>;</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">export</span> <span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">middleware</span>(<span class="params"><span class="attr">request</span>: <span class="title class_">NextRequest</span></span>) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> { pathname } = request.<span class="property">nextUrl</span>;</span><br><span class="line"> </span><br><span class="line"> <span class="comment">// 1. 重定向 / 重写</span></span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">if</span> (pathname === <span class="string">'/old-page'</span>) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">return</span> <span class="title class_">NextResponse</span>.<span class="title function_">redirect</span>(<span class="keyword">new</span> <span class="title function_">URL</span>(<span class="string">'/new-page'</span>, request.<span class="property">url</span>));</span><br><span class="line"> }</span><br><span class="line"> </span><br><span class="line"> <span class="comment">// 2. 国际化（i18n）</span></span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> locale = request.<span class="property">cookies</span>.<span class="title function_">get</span>(<span class="string">'locale'</span>)?.<span class="property">value</span> || <span class="string">'zh'</span>;</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">if</span> (!pathname.<span class="title function_">startsWith</span>(<span class="string">`/<span class="subst">${locale}</span>`</span>)) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">return</span> <span class="title class_">NextResponse</span>.<span class="title function_">rewrite</span>(<span class="keyword">new</span> <span class="title function_">URL</span>(<span class="string">`/<span class="subst">${locale}</span><span class="subst">${pathname}</span>`</span>, request.<span class="property">url</span>));</span><br><span class="line"> }</span><br><span class="line"> </span><br><span class="line"> <span class="comment">// 3. 认证 + 授权</span></span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> token = request.<span class="property">cookies</span>.<span class="title function_">get</span>(<span class="string">'session'</span>)?.<span class="property">value</span>;</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">if</span> (!token && pathname.<span class="title function_">startsWith</span>(<span class="string">'/dashboard'</span>)) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">return</span> <span class="title class_">NextResponse</span>.<span class="title function_">redirect</span>(<span class="keyword">new</span> <span class="title function_">URL</span>(<span class="string">'/login'</span>, request.<span class="property">url</span>));</span><br><span class="line"> }</span><br><span class="line"> </span><br><span class="line"> <span class="comment">// 4. A/B 测试</span></span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> experiment = <span class="title class_">Math</span>.<span class="title function_">random</span>() > <span class="number">0.5</span> ? <span class="string">'a'</span> : <span class="string">'b'</span>;</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> response = <span class="title class_">NextResponse</span>.<span class="title function_">next</span>();</span><br><span class="line"> response.<span class="property">headers</span>.<span class="title function_">set</span>(<span class="string">'x-experiment'</span>, experiment);</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">return</span> response;</span><br><span class="line">}</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 匹配规则：只对特定路径执行中间件</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">export</span> <span class="keyword">const</span> config = {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="attr">matcher</span>: [</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="string">'/((?!api|_next/static|_next/image|favicon.ico).*)'</span>,</span><br><span class="line"> ],</span><br><span class="line">};</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>生产使用场景</strong>：</p> <table> <thead> <tr> <th>场景</th> <th>实现方式</th> <th>注意</th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr> <td>认证拦截</td> <td>检查 token/ session cookie，无则重定向</td> <td>不要在 Middleware 中解密 JWT（Edge Runtime 性能有限）</td> </tr> <tr> <td>A/B 测试</td> <td>读取 Cookie 或随机分配</td> <td>确保同一用户始终看到同一版本</td> </tr> <tr> <td>国际化重定向</td> <td>根据 Accept-Language 或 Cookie 重写 URL</td> <td>配合 <code>rewrite</code> 而非 <code>redirect</code></td> </tr> <tr> <td>流量控制</td> <td>基于 IP 的速率限制</td> <td>Edge Runtime 限制需用外部 KV 存储</td> </tr> <tr> <td>SEO 优化</td> <td>301 重定向、规范 URL 处理</td> <td>避免链式重定向</td> </tr> <tr> <td>Feature Flag</td> <td>读取 KV 存储的旗标值</td> <td>避免在每个请求中查询数据库</td> </tr> </tbody></table> <p><strong>中间件的限制</strong>：</p> <ul> <li>运行在 Edge Runtime（不支持 Node.js API）</li> <li>执行时间限制（Vercel Free Plan 30s，Pro 300s）</li> <li>无法读取本地文件系统</li> <li>大量计算会退化边缘性能</li> </ul> <p><strong>面试金句</strong>：Middleware 是在”路由匹配之前”的最后一个拦截点——适合做全局性的请求预处理，但不适合做数据获取或重型计算。记住：中间件执行在 Edge，数据库查询在 Server。</p> <p>参考：<a href="https://nextjs.org/docs/app/building-your-application/routing/middleware">Next.js Middleware</a></p> <hr> <h3 id="27-Next-js-图片优化与-CLS（Cumulative-Layout-Shift）优化"><a href="#27-Next-js-图片优化与-CLS（Cumulative-Layout-Shift）优化" class="headerlink" title="27. Next.js 图片优化与 CLS（Cumulative Layout Shift）优化"></a>27. Next.js 图片优化与 CLS（Cumulative Layout Shift）优化</h3><p><strong>标准答案</strong>：</p> <p><strong>Next.js Image 组件的最佳实践</strong>：</p> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br><span class="line">12</span><br><span class="line">19</span><br><span class="line">20</span><br><span class="line">21</span><br><span class="line">22</span><br><span class="line">23</span><br><span class="line">24</span><br><span class="line">25</span><br><span class="line">26</span><br><span class="line">27</span><br><span class="line">28</span><br><span class="line">29</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line"><span class="keyword">import</span> <span class="title class_">Image</span> <span class="keyword">from</span> <span class="string">'next/image'</span>;</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 基础用法（自动优化 + 懒加载）</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><<span class="string">"Hero"</span></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="tag"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="attr">width</span>=<span class="string">{1200}</span></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="tag"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="attr">height</span>=<span class="string">{600}</span> // <span class="language-xml"> <span class="attr">priority</span> // <span class="attr">首屏图片加上</span> <span class="attr">priority</span>，<span class="attr">跳过懒加载</span></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="tag"><span class="language-xml">/></span></span></span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 远程图片（需要配置域名）</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// next.config.ts</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">const</span> config = {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="attr">images</span>: {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="attr">remotePatterns</span>: [</span><br><span class="line"> { <span class="attr">protocol</span>: <span class="string">'https'</span>, <span class="attr">hostname</span>: <span class="string">'cdn.example.com'</span> },</span><br><span class="line"> ],</span><br><span class="line"> },</span><br><span class="line">};</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 响应式图片</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><<span class="name">Image</span></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="tag"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="attr">src</span>=<span class="string">{src}</span></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="tag"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="attr">alt</span>=<span class="string">"Responsive"</span></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="tag"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="attr">sizes</span>=<span class="string">"(max-width: 768px) 100vw, (max-width: 1200px) 50vw, 33vw"</span></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="tag"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="attr">fill</span> // <span class="attr">父元素需设置</span> <span class="attr">position:</span> <span class="attr">relative</span> + <span class="attr">宽高</span></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="tag"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="attr">style</span>=<span class="string">{{</span> <span class="attr">objectFit:</span> '<span class="attr">cover</span>' }}</span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="tag"><span class="language-xml">/></span></span></span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong><code>next/image</code> 做了什么？</strong></p> <ol> <li><strong>自动 WebP/AVIF 转换</strong> — 根据浏览器支持选择最优格式</li> <li><strong>响应式图片</strong> — 设备尺寸不同时生成不同分辨率</li> <li><strong>懒加载</strong> — 默认 <code>loading="lazy"</code>，进入视口才加载</li> <li><strong>防止 CLS</strong> — 自动设置宽高比，避免图片加载后页面跳动</li> <li><strong>占位图</strong> — <code>placeholder="blur"</code> 基于 blurDataURL 显示模糊缩略图</li> </ol> <p><strong>CLS 优化的系统方法</strong>：</p> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br><span class="line">12</span><br><span class="line">13</span><br><span class="line">14</span><br><span class="line">15</span><br><span class="line">16</span><br><span class="line">17</span><br><span class="line">18</span><br><span class="line">19</span><br><span class="line">20</span><br><span class="line">21</span><br><span class="line">22</span><br><span class="line">23</span><br><span class="line">24</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 1. 所有图片显式指定宽高</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// ❌ 不指定 → CLS</span></span><br><span class="line"><div style={{ <span class="attr">backgroundImage</span>: <span class="string">`url(<span class="subst">${src}</span>)`</span> }} /></span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// ✅ 指定宽高 → 浏览器预留空间</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><<span class="name">Image</span> <span class="attr">src</span>=<span class="string">{src}</span> <span class="attr">width</span>=<span class="string">{800}</span> <span class="attr">height</span>=<span class="string">{450}</span> <span class="attr">alt</span>=<span class="string">""</span> /></span></span></span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 2. 自定义宽高比容器（非 Image 组件时）</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><<span class="name">div</span> <span class="attr">style</span>=<span class="string">{{</span> <span class="attr">aspectRatio:</span> '<span class="attr">16</span>/<span class="attr">9</span>', <span class="attr">position:</span> '<span class="attr">relative</span>' }}></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"><<span class="name">img</span> <span class="attr">src</span>=<span class="string">{src}</span> <span class="attr">style</span>=<span class="string">{{</span> <span class="attr">width:</span> '<span class="attr">100</span>%', <span class="attr">height:</span> '<span class="attr">100</span>%', <span class="attr">objectFit:</span> '<span class="attr">cover</span>' }} /></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"></<span class="name">div</span>></span></span></span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 3. 首屏图片使用 priority 跳过懒加载</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// ❌ 无 priority → 首屏图片可能有延迟</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><<span class="name">Image</span> <span class="attr">src</span>=<span class="string">{hero}</span> <span class="attr">alt</span>=<span class="string">"Hero"</span> /></span></span></span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// ✅ priority → 被视作关键资源预加载</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><<span class="name">Image</span> <span class="attr">src</span>=<span class="string">{hero}</span> <span class="attr">alt</span>=<span class="string">"Hero"</span> <span class="attr">priority</span> /></span></span></span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 4. 字体显示控制</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 使用 next/font 自动优化（无 FOIT/FOUT）</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">import</span> { <span class="title class_">Inter</span> } <span class="keyword">from</span> <span class="string">'next/font/google'</span>;</span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">const</span> inter = <span class="title class_">Inter</span>({ <span class="attr">subsets</span>: [<span class="string">'latin'</span>] });</span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 在 layout 中 <body className={inter.className}></span></span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>生产 CLS 调试 checklist</strong>：</p> <figure class="highlight txt"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line">□ 所有 <img>/<Image> 指定宽高</span><br><span class="line">□ 首屏图片加 priority</span><br><span class="line">□ 静态资源用 blur placeholder</span><br><span class="line">□ 使用 next/font 替代 <link> 加载字体</span><br><span class="line">□ 动态内容（广告/嵌入）预留占位</span><br><span class="line">□ Suspense fallback 包含骨架屏（预留尺寸）</span><br><span class="line">□ 动画和过渡使用 transform（不触发 layout）</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>面试金句</strong>：Next.js Image 组件不仅仅是”图片优化”——它本质上是一个 <strong>CLS 消除器</strong>。通过强制指定宽高比（<code>width</code> + <code>height</code>）和 <code>sizes</code> 属性，它确保浏览器在图片下载前就知道预留空间大小，这是 Web Vital 中 CLS 得分的关键因素。</p> <p>参考：<a href="https://nextjs.org/docs/app/building-your-application/optimizing/images">Next.js Image Optimization</a></p> <hr> <h2 id="0x0A-React-性能优化（2026-版）"><a href="#0x0A-React-性能优化（2026-版）" class="headerlink" title="0x0A React 性能优化（2026 版）"></a>0x0A React 性能优化（2026 版）</h2><h3 id="28-useMemo-useCallback-React-memo-到底什么时候该用、什么时候不该用？"><a href="#28-useMemo-useCallback-React-memo-到底什么时候该用、什么时候不该用？" class="headerlink" title="28. useMemo / useCallback / React.memo 到底什么时候该用、什么时候不该用？"></a>28. useMemo / useCallback / React.memo 到底什么时候该用、什么时候不该用？</h3><p><strong>标准答案</strong>：</p> <p><strong>通用原则：不用白不用？错！这些 API 本身有开销——多用多错。</strong></p> <p><strong>应该在什么时候用？</strong></p> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br><span class="line">12</span><br><span class="line">13</span><br><span class="line">14</span><br><span class="line">15</span><br><span class="line">16</span><br><span class="line">17</span><br><span class="line">18</span><br><span class="line">19</span><br><span class="line">20</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line"><span class="comment">// ✅ 应该用：昂贵的计算</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">const</span> sortedList = <span class="title function_">useMemo</span>(<span class="function">() =></span> {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">return</span> hugeList.<span class="title function_">sort</span>(<span class="function">(<span class="params">a, b</span>) =></span> <span class="title function_">expensiveCompare</span>(a, b));</span><br><span class="line">}, [hugeList]);</span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 如果 hugeList 没变，跳过排序。排序本身 O(n log n)，值得缓存。</span></span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// ✅ 应该用：引用稳定性（配合 React.memo）</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">Parent</span>(<span class="params"></span>) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> config = <span class="title function_">useMemo</span>(<span class="function">() =></span> ({ <span class="attr">theme</span>: <span class="string">'dark'</span>, <span class="attr">lang</span>: <span class="string">'zh'</span> }), []);</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="comment">// 稳定引用 → 子组件的 memo 能正常工作</span></span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">return</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><<span class="name">Child</span> <span class="attr">config</span>=<span class="string">{config}</span> /></span></span>;</span><br><span class="line">}</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// ✅ 应该用：useCallback 避免子组件不必要渲染</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">Parent</span>(<span class="params"></span>) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> handleClick = <span class="title function_">useCallback</span>(<span class="function">() =></span> {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="title function_">trackEvent</span>(<span class="string">'click'</span>);</span><br><span class="line"> }, []); <span class="comment">// 稳定函数引用</span></span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">return</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><<span class="name">MemoButton</span> <span class="attr">onClick</span>=<span class="string">{handleClick}</span>></span>Click<span class="tag"></<span class="name">MemoButton</span>></span></span>;</span><br><span class="line">}</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>不应该在什么时候用？</strong></p> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br><span class="line">12</span><br><span class="line">13</span><br><span class="line">14</span><br><span class="line">15</span><br><span class="line">16</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line"><span class="comment">// ❌ 不该用：简单计算，useMemo 本身开销更大</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">const</span> total = <span class="title function_">useMemo</span>(<span class="function">() =></span> a + b, [a, b]); <span class="comment">// 加法才几纳秒！对比依赖数组检查的开销</span></span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// ❌ 不该用：作为"默认值"缓存（useMemo 在大多数渲染中执行了函数）</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">const</span> data = <span class="title function_">useMemo</span>(<span class="function">() =></span> <span class="title function_">fetchInitialData</span>(), []); <span class="comment">// 用 useEffect + useState 替代</span></span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// ❌ 不该用：花式绕过闭包——直接修代码逻辑</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">const</span> onSubmit = <span class="title function_">useCallback</span>(<span class="function">(<span class="params">e</span>) =></span> {</span><br><span class="line"> e.<span class="title function_">preventDefault</span>();</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="title function_">setForm</span>(<span class="function"><span class="params">prev</span> =></span> ({ ...prev, [e.<span class="property">target</span>.<span class="property">name</span>]: e.<span class="property">target</span>.<span class="property">value</span> }));</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="comment">// ↑ 用函数式更新替代依赖</span></span><br><span class="line">}, []); <span class="comment">// 依赖空数组但引用了外部变量？这是 Bug！</span></span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// ❌ 不该用：所有函数都包裹 useCallback</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><<span class="name">button</span> <span class="attr">onClick</span>=<span class="string">{useCallback(()</span> =></span> console.log('hi'), [])}>Hi<span class="tag"></<span class="name">button</span>></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 原生 button 不关心引用变化，useCallback 无意义还增加内存</span></span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>决策树</strong>：</p> <figure class="highlight txt"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br><span class="line">12</span><br><span class="line">13</span><br><span class="line">14</span><br><span class="line">15</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line">是否需要缓存？</span><br><span class="line">├── 计算（useMemo）</span><br><span class="line">│ ├── O(n) 以上复杂计算？ → 用</span><br><span class="line">│ ├── 简单计算/字面量 → 别用</span><br><span class="line">│ └── 对象/数组引用稳定性？ → 用（配合 React.memo）</span><br><span class="line">│</span><br><span class="line">├── 函数（useCallback）</span><br><span class="line">│ ├── 传给 React.memo 子组件？ → 用</span><br><span class="line">│ ├── 传给 useEffect 依赖？ → 用</span><br><span class="line">│ └── 传给原生 DOM 元素？ → 别用</span><br><span class="line">│</span><br><span class="line">└── 组件（React.memo）</span><br><span class="line"> ├── 纯展示组件 + props 浅比较稳定？ → 用</span><br><span class="line"> ├── props 每次变化（如传新对象）？ → 别用</span><br><span class="line"> └── 不确定？ → 先用 Profiler 测量，再决定</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>深入思考</strong>：</p> <ul> <li><strong>React.memo 的”反模式”</strong>：如果父组件每次都传新对象 <code>{ config: { theme } }</code>，即使子组件 <code>React.memo</code> 了，浅比较也会失败。必须先 <code>useMemo</code> 稳定对象引用</li> <li><strong>性能测量的唯一标准</strong>：永远先用 Profiler 定位真实瓶颈，不要凭感觉加 memo</li> <li><strong>React Compiler 的替代</strong>：如果项目已经使用了 React Compiler，编译器会自动为你处理这些优化——你不需要手动写 <code>useMemo</code>/<code>useCallback</code>/<code>React.memo</code></li> </ul> <p>参考：<a href="https://kentcdodds.com/blog/usememo-and-usecallback">When to useMemo and useCallback</a></p> <hr> <h3 id="29-并发模式（Concurrent-Mode）深入实践：useTransition-useDeferredValue-startTransition"><a href="#29-并发模式（Concurrent-Mode）深入实践：useTransition-useDeferredValue-startTransition" class="headerlink" title="29. 并发模式（Concurrent Mode）深入实践：useTransition / useDeferredValue / startTransition"></a>29. 并发模式（Concurrent Mode）深入实践：useTransition / useDeferredValue / startTransition</h3><p><strong>标准答案</strong>：</p> <p>并发模式的核心思想是”<strong>React 可以同时准备多个版本的 UI，并在合适的时机展示最相关的那个</strong>“。</p> <p><strong>三个 API 的区别</strong>：</p> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br><span class="line">12</span><br><span class="line">13</span><br><span class="line">14</span><br><span class="line">15</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 1. startTransition — 声明低优先级更新</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">import</span> { startTransition } <span class="keyword">from</span> <span class="string">'react'</span>;</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="title function_">setInput</span>(value); <span class="comment">// 高优：立即更新输入框</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="title function_">startTransition</span>(<span class="function">() =></span> {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="title function_">setSearchResults</span>(<span class="title function_">filter</span>(value)); <span class="comment">// 低优：可被中断</span></span><br><span class="line">});</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 2. useTransition — 带 pending 状态的 startTransition</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">const</span> [isPending, startTransition] = <span class="title function_">useTransition</span>();</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 3. useDeferredValue — 让一个值"滞后"</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">const</span> deferredQuery = <span class="title function_">useDeferredValue</span>(query);</span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// query 变化 → 输入框立即更新</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// deferredQuery 变化 → UI 延迟更新（React 有空时才更新）</span></span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>什么时候用哪个？</strong></p> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span 场景 A：搜索输入（用 useTransition）</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">SearchPage</span>(<span class="params"></span>) {</span><br><span (</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><></span></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"><<span <th>API</th> <th>控制权</th> <th>适用场景</th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr> <td><code>startTransition</code></td> <td>你决定哪个更新是低优先级的</td> <td>你自己可以控制 setState</td> </tr> <tr> <td><code>useDeferredValue</code></td> <td>你 defer 一个值，React 决定何时更新</td> <td>值来自外部（props、第三方 Hook）</td> </tr> <tr> <td><code>useTransition</code></td> <td><code>startTransition</code> + <code>isPending</code></td> <td>需要显示 pending 状态</td> </tr> </tbody></table> <p><strong>并发模式最佳实践 2026</strong>：</p> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="comment">// 高优：用户直接交互的区域</span></span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">const</span> [tab, setTab] = <span class="title
