class="name">div</span>></span></span></span><br><span class="line"> );</span><br><span class="line">}</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>深入思考</strong>：</p> <ul> <li><strong><code>useTransition</code> 可能永远不会触发 pending 状态</strong>：如果低优先更新在 5ms 内完成，React 可能直接在同步帧内完成，不展示 pending</li> <li><strong><code>useDeferredValue</code> 的 timeout 问题</strong>：deferred 的值可能在用户停止交互后仍然”延迟”——这通常是期望行为（优先响应用户操作），但需注意 UX</li> <li><strong>并发模式不等于”异步”</strong>：所有更新仍然是”同步”执行的，并发模式的”中断”发生在 Fiber 树构建层面，不是 JS 层面的多线程</li> </ul> <p>参考：<a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://react.dev/reference/react/useTransition">React Concurrent Features</a></p> <hr> <h3 id="30-虚拟列表选型：react-window-vs-tanstack-react-virtual-vs-react-virtuoso"><a href="#30-虚拟列表选型：react-window-vs-tanstack-react-virtual-vs-react-virtuoso" class="headerlink" title="30. 虚拟列表选型：react-window vs @tanstack/react-virtual vs react-virtuoso"></a>30. 虚拟列表选型：react-window vs @tanstack/react-virtual vs react-virtuoso</h3><p><strong>标准答案</strong>：</p> <p>长列表渲染是 React 性能瓶颈最常见场景之一。虚拟列表的核心理念是”只渲染视口内可见的元素”。</p> <p><strong>2026 年三大虚拟列表库对比</strong>：</p> <table> <thead> <tr> <th>维度</th> <th>react-window</th> <th>@tanstack/react-virtual</th> <th>react-virtuoso</th> </tr> </thead> <tbody><tr> <td><strong>包体积</strong></td> <td>~20KB</td> <td>~10KB (headless)</td> <td>~25KB</td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>动态高度</strong></td> <td>❌ 需手动计算</td> <td>✅ 自动</td> <td>✅ 自动</td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>分组/Sticky Header</strong></td> <td>❌</td> <td>❌（需自行实现）</td> <td>✅ 内置</td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>无限滚动</strong></td> <td>❌</td> <td>❌</td> <td>✅ 内置</td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>Table 虚拟化</strong></td> <td>❌</td> <td>✅ (结合 flex)</td> <td>✅</td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>Grid 虚拟化</strong></td> <td>✅ (FixedSizeGrid)</td> <td>❌（需自行封装）</td> <td>✅</td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>滚动到索引</strong></td> <td>✅</td> <td>✅</td> <td>✅</td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>TypeScript</strong></td> <td>✅</td> <td>✅ 极佳</td> <td>✅</td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>维护状态</strong></td> <td>维护模式</td> <td>活跃（TanStack 生态）</td> <td>活跃</td> </tr> <tr> <td><strong>下载量/周</strong></td> <td>~3.5M</td> <td>~1.3M</td> <td>~2.1M</td> </tr> </tbody></table> <p><strong>选型建议</strong>：</p> <figure class="highlight txt"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br><span class="line">11</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line">简单需求（固定高度、列表型）</span><br><span class="line">→ react-window：成熟简单、生态完善</span><br><span class="line">→ 代码：<FixedSizeList height={600} itemCount={10000} itemSize={50}></span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line">中等需求（动态高度、scroll recovery）</span><br><span class="line">→ @tanstack/react-virtual：灵活、TypeScript 友好</span><br><span class="line">→ 代码：useVirtualizer({ count: 10000, estimateSize: () => 50 })</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line">复杂需求（分组、sticky header、无限滚动、表格）</span><br><span class="line">→ react-virtuoso：开箱即用</span><br><span class="line">→ 代码：<Virtuoso totalCount={10000} itemContent={index => <Row index={index} />}></span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>@tanstack/react-virtual 2026 生产代码</strong>：</p> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span scroll 事件数量需特别关注</li> <li><strong><code>directDomUpdates</code> 选项</strong>：@tanstack/react-virtual 3.x 支持 <code>directDomUpdates: true</code>，跳过 React reconciler 直接操作 DOM，对超高频滚动（30fps+）有显著性能提升</li> <li><strong>白屏闪烁</strong>：快速滚动时可能看到空区域，通过调大 <code>overscan</code> 缓解（trade-off: 渲染更多元素）</li> </ul> <p>参考：<a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://tanstack.com/virtual/v3">TanStack Virtual</a> | class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 2. 组件级代码分割（谨慎使用——只对大体量组件）</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">const</span> <span class="title class="line"><span class="comment">// 3. 条件渲染懒加载</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">function</span> <span class="title function_">PhotoViewer</span>(<span class="params">{ photoId }: { photoId: <span class="built_in">string</span> }</span>) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">return</span> (</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><<span class="name">Suspense</span> <span class="attr">fallback</span>=<span class="string">{</span><<span class="attr">PhotoSkeleton</span> /></span>}></span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="language-xml"> <span class="tag"><<span class="name">PhotoDetail</span> <span class="attr">id</span>=<span class="string">{photoId}</span> <span class="title function_">PhotoLink</span>(<span class="params">{ photoId, children }: <span class="title class_">Props</span></span>) {</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="keyword">return</span> (</span><br><span class="line"> <span class="language-xml"><span class="tag"><<span class="name">Link</span> <span class="attr">to</span>=<span class="string">{</span>`/<span class="attr">photo</span>/${<span class="attr">photoId</span>}`} <span class="attr">onMouseEnter</span>=<span class="tag"></<span class="name">Link</span>></span></span></span><br><span class="line"> );</span><br><span class="line">}</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>Bundle 分析最佳实践</strong>：</p> <figure class="highlight bash"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">10</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line"><span class="comment"># 1. 可视化分析</span></span><br><span class="line">npx next-bundle-analyzer <span class="comment"># Next.js 项目</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment"># 或</span></span><br><span class="line">npm install --save-dev vite-bundle-visualizer <span class="comment"># Vite 项目</span></span><br><span class="line">npx vite-bundle-visualizer</span><br><span class="line"></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment"># 2. 关注指标</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment"># ✅ 首屏 JS < 150KB（压缩后）</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment"># ✅ 路由级 chunk < 50KB</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment"># ✅ 没有重复依赖（检查 lodash、moment 等大库）</span></span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>2026 年 Bundle 优化前沿</strong>：</p> <figure class="highlight tsx"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line"><span class="comment">// 5. React.lazy + Error Boundary + Suspense（完整兜底）</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">import</span> { lazy, <span class="title class_">Suspense</span> } <span class="keyword">from</span> <span class="string">'react'</span>;</span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">import</span> { <span class="title class_">ErrorBoundary</span> } <span class_">HeavyWidget</span> = <span class="title function_">lazy</span>(<span class="function">() =></span> <span class="keyword">import</span>(<span 动态 import + 命名导出</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="keyword">const</span> <span class="title class_">HeavyComponent</span> = <span class="title function_">lazy</span>(<span Preload 策略：使用 React 19 的 preload API（可选）</span></span><br><span class="line"><span class="comment">// <link rel="preload" as="script" href="/chunk-heavy.js" /></span></span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>常用优化 checklist</strong>：</p> <figure class="highlight txt"><table><tr><td class="gutter"><pre><span class="line">1</span><br><span class="line">2</span><br><span class="line">3</span><br><span class="line">4</span><br><span class="line">5</span><br><span class="line">6</span><br><span class="line">7</span><br><span class="line">8</span><br><span class="line">9</span><br></pre></td><td class="code"><pre><span class="line">□ 路由级代码分割 → 每个路由一个 chunk</span><br><span class="line">□ 第三方库按需导入 → 只 import 你用的函数</span><br><span class="line"> lodash/moment → dayjs/date-fns（tree-shakable）</span><br><span class="line">□ 大图懒加载 → next/image + lazy loading</span><br><span class="line">□ 动态 import 大组件 → Suspense + fallback</span><br><span class="line">□ profiler 定位重渲染 → 减少不必要的更新</span><br><span class="line">□ 移除未使用的 polyfill → core-js 按需</span><br><span class="line">□ 压缩 JS 资源 → Gzip / Brotli（各 CDN 自动）</span><br><span class="line">□ 关键 CSS 内联 → 非关键 CSS 异步加载</span><br></pre></td></tr></table></figure> <p><strong>面试金句</strong>：Bundle 优化的第一原则是”衡量两次、切割一次”——先用 Bundle Analyzer 确定瓶颈在哪儿（是第三方库过大还是业务代码未分割），再针对性优化。对于大多数项目，<strong>路由级代码分割 + 大库替换为轻量级替代</strong> 这两步就能解决 80% 的 bundle 问题。</p> <hr> <blockquote> <p>本文将持续更新。</p> </blockquote> </div> <footer class="post-footer"> <div
